// ============================================================================
// SYSTEM KONTROL MASTER STEAMBOX & MONITOR OUTDOOR (30 UNIT) - STATIC TAG ONLY
// Trigger: Timer 1 Detik (1000ms)
// ============================================================================

// 1. Ekstrak Waktu Sistem (Format HH:MM:SS)
var waktuSekarangString = ("0" + ($Hour || 0)).slice(-2) + ":" + ("0" + ($Minute || 0)).slice(-2) + ":" + ("0" + ($Second || 0)).slice(-2);
var totalDetikSekarang = (($Hour || 0) * 3600) + (($Minute || 0) * 60) + ($Second || 0);

// 2. Auto-Inisialisasi / Tulis Default ke Tag HMI jika Kosong (Agar bisa diedit dari Layar SCADA)
$Sys_Control.txt_status_kosong = $Sys_Control.txt_status_kosong || "STEAMBOX KOSONG";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_preheat = $Sys_Control.txt_status_preheat || "SEDANG PEMANASAN";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_pemanasan = $Sys_Control.txt_status_pemanasan || "MENUNGGU MENDIDIH (< 100 C)";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_pemasakan = $Sys_Control.txt_status_pemasakan || "SEDANG MEMASAK (MENDIDIH)";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_selesai = $Sys_Control.txt_status_selesai || "PROSES SELESAI - SILAKAN KOSONGKAN TANGKI";
$Sys_Control.txt_selesai_preheat = $Sys_Control.txt_selesai_preheat || "PEMANASAN SELESAI - STEAMBOX SIAP UNTUK PEMASAKAN";
$Sys_Control.txt_siap_preheat = $Sys_Control.txt_siap_preheat || "SIAP PEMANASAN - SILAKAN TEKAN START";
$Sys_Control.txt_siap_cooking = $Sys_Control.txt_siap_cooking || "RESEP TERPASANG - SILAKAN TEKAN START";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_resep = $Sys_Control.txt_status_resep || "RESEP TERPASANG - SILAKAN TEKAN START";
$Sys_Control.txt_preheat_paused = $Sys_Control.txt_preheat_paused || "PRE-HEAT DIHENTIKAN (PAUSED)";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_paused = $Sys_Control.txt_status_paused || "MESIN BERHENTI (PAUSED)";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_maintenance = $Sys_Control.txt_status_maintenance || "MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_offline = $Sys_Control.txt_status_offline || "KONEKSI OFFLINE (MCB TRIP/ALAT MATI)";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_disable = $Sys_Control.txt_status_disable || "UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI";
$Sys_Control.txt_status_sensor_error = $Sys_Control.txt_status_sensor_error || "ERROR SENSOR (OPENLOOP/HHHH)";
$Sys_Control.txt_sensor_error = $Sys_Control.txt_sensor_error || "proses memasak, tetapi sensor error, cek segera !";

// 3. Teks Status dari HMI untuk dibaca oleh skrip unit
var txtKosong = $Sys_Control.txt_status_kosong;
var txtPreheat = $Sys_Control.txt_status_preheat;
var txtPemanasan = $Sys_Control.txt_status_pemanasan;
var txtPemasakan = $Sys_Control.txt_status_pemasakan;
var txtSelesai = $Sys_Control.txt_status_selesai;
var txtSelesaiPreheat = $Sys_Control.txt_selesai_preheat;
var txtSiapPreheat = $Sys_Control.txt_siap_preheat;
var txtSiapCooking = $Sys_Control.txt_siap_cooking;
var txtStatusResep = $Sys_Control.txt_status_resep;
var txtPreheatPaused = $Sys_Control.txt_preheat_paused;
var txtPaused = $Sys_Control.txt_status_paused;
var txtMaintenance = $Sys_Control.txt_status_maintenance;
var txtOffline = $Sys_Control.txt_status_offline;
var txtDisable = $Sys_Control.txt_status_disable;
var txtSensorError = $Sys_Control.txt_status_sensor_error;
var txtSensorErrorCooking = $Sys_Control.txt_sensor_error;
var tempErrorLimit = $Sys_Control.temp_error_limit || 30000;

// Array penampung unit yang sedang memasak untuk monitor luar
var runningRooms = [];

// Helper function format durasi
function formatTime(totalSeconds) {
    var h = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 3600);
    var m = Math.floor((totalSeconds % 3600) / 60);
    var s = totalSeconds % 60;
    return ("0" + h).slice(-2) + ":" + ("0" + m).slice(-2) + ":" + ("0" + s).slice(-2);
}

// Helper function estimasi jam selesai
function getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, sisa) {
    var est = (totalDetikSekarang + sisa) % 86400;
    var he = Math.floor(est / 3600);
    var me = Math.floor((est % 3600) / 60);
    var se = est % 60;
    return ("0" + he).slice(-2) + ":" + ("0" + me).slice(-2) + ":" + ("0" + se).slice(-2);
}


// 3. Reset Global Trigger Log (Untuk Data Group Log_Steambox)
if ($Sys_Control.trigger_log) {
    $Sys_Control.trigger_log = false;
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 1
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_1.reset) {
    $sb_1.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_1.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_1.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_1.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_1.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_1.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_1.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_1.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_1.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_1.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_1.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_1.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.1 = "";
    $recipe_nama.1 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.1 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.1 = "";
    $recipe_qty.1 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.1 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.1 = "";
    
    $sb_1.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_1.status_resep = false;
    $sb_1.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_1.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_1.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_1.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_1 = 0;
    var activeSisa_1 = $sb_1.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_1 = $sb_1.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_1.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_1 = $sb_1.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_1 = activeSisa_1 + adjustSecs_1;
        if (activeSisa_1 < 0) {
            activeSisa_1 = 0;
        }
        $sb_1.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_1;
        
        activePerubahan_1 = activePerubahan_1 + $sb_1.adjust_menit;
        $sb_1.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_1;
        $sb_1.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb1._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_1.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_1.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_1.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_1.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_1.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb1._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_1.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_1 = ($sb1.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb1.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_1.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_1.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_1.mode_preheat || $sb_1.status_resep) {
                        $sb_1.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_1.mode_preheat && !$sb_1.status_resep && $sb_1.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_1 === 0 && !$sb_1.status_selesai && $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_1.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_1.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_1.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_1.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_1.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_1.status_kosong && !$sb_1.status_selesai && !$sb_1.mode_preheat && !$sb_1.status_resep) {
                        $sb_1.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_1.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_1.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_1.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_1.status_resep && activeSisa_1 === 0) {
                                $sb_1.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_1.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_1.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_1.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_1);
                        scale_up_1 = ((($sb_1.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_1) * 60) - activeSisa_1;
                        $sb_1.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_1 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_1);
                        if ($sb_1.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_1);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_1.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_1.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_1.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_1.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_1.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_1.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_1.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_1.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_1.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_1.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_1.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_1.suhu_awal = $sb1.temp;
                            activePerubahan_1 = 0;
                            $sb_1.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_1.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb1.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb1.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_1.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_1.suhu_akhir = $sb1.temp;
                            $sb_1.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_1.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_1.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_1.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_1.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_1.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_1.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_1 = $sb_1.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_1.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_1;
                            $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_1.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_1.suhu_awal = $sb1.temp;
                            activePerubahan_1 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_1.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb1.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_1.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_1.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_1.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_1.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_1.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_1);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_1 = ((($sb_1.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_1) * 60) - activeSisa_1) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_1;
                            $sb_1.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_1.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_1);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 1, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_1,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_1.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_1.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_1.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_1.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_1.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_1.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_1 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_1 = activeSisa_1 - 1;
                                $sb_1.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_1;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_1);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_1 = ((($sb_1.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_1) * 60) - activeSisa_1) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_1;
                            $sb_1.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_1 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_1 = 0;
                                $sb_1.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_1.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_1) * 60);
                                $sb_1.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb1.temp;
                                $sb_1.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb1.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_1.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_1.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_1.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 1;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.1;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.1;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.1;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.1;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.1;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.1;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.1;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_1.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_1.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_1.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_1.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_1; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_1.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_1.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_1);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 1, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_1,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_1.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_1.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_1) {
                    $sb_1.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb1.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_1.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_1.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_1.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_1.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_1.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_1.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_1.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_1.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_1.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_1.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_1.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 2
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_2.reset) {
    $sb_2.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_2.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_2.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_2.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_2.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_2.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_2.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_2.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_2.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_2.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_2.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_2.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.2 = "";
    $recipe_nama.2 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.2 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.2 = "";
    $recipe_qty.2 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.2 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.2 = "";
    
    $sb_2.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_2.status_resep = false;
    $sb_2.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_2.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_2.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_2.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_2 = 0;
    var activeSisa_2 = $sb_2.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_2 = $sb_2.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_2.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_2 = $sb_2.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_2 = activeSisa_2 + adjustSecs_2;
        if (activeSisa_2 < 0) {
            activeSisa_2 = 0;
        }
        $sb_2.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_2;
        
        activePerubahan_2 = activePerubahan_2 + $sb_2.adjust_menit;
        $sb_2.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_2;
        $sb_2.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb2._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_2.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_2.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_2.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_2.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_2.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb2._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_2.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_2 = ($sb2.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb2.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_2.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_2.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_2.mode_preheat || $sb_2.status_resep) {
                        $sb_2.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_2.mode_preheat && !$sb_2.status_resep && $sb_2.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_2 === 0 && !$sb_2.status_selesai && $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_2.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_2.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_2.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_2.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_2.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_2.status_kosong && !$sb_2.status_selesai && !$sb_2.mode_preheat && !$sb_2.status_resep) {
                        $sb_2.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_2.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_2.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_2.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_2.status_resep && activeSisa_2 === 0) {
                                $sb_2.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_2.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_2.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_2.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_2);
                        scale_up_2 = ((($sb_2.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_2) * 60) - activeSisa_2;
                        $sb_2.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_2 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_2);
                        if ($sb_2.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_2);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_2.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_2.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_2.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_2.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_2.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_2.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_2.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_2.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_2.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_2.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_2.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_2.suhu_awal = $sb2.temp;
                            activePerubahan_2 = 0;
                            $sb_2.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_2.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb2.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb2.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_2.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_2.suhu_akhir = $sb2.temp;
                            $sb_2.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_2.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_2.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_2.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_2.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_2.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_2.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_2 = $sb_2.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_2.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_2;
                            $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_2.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_2.suhu_awal = $sb2.temp;
                            activePerubahan_2 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_2.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb2.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_2.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_2.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_2.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_2.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_2.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_2);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_2 = ((($sb_2.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_2) * 60) - activeSisa_2) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_2;
                            $sb_2.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_2.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_2);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 2, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_2,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_2.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_2.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_2.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_2.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_2.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_2.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_2 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_2 = activeSisa_2 - 1;
                                $sb_2.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_2;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_2);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_2 = ((($sb_2.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_2) * 60) - activeSisa_2) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_2;
                            $sb_2.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_2 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_2 = 0;
                                $sb_2.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_2.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_2) * 60);
                                $sb_2.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb2.temp;
                                $sb_2.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb2.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_2.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_2.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_2.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 2;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.2;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.2;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.2;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.2;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.2;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.2;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.2;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_2.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_2.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_2.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_2.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_2; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_2.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_2.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_2);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 2, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_2,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_2.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_2.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_2) {
                    $sb_2.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb2.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_2.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_2.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_2.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_2.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_2.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_2.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_2.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_2.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_2.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_2.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_2.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 3
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_3.reset) {
    $sb_3.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_3.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_3.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_3.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_3.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_3.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_3.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_3.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_3.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_3.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_3.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_3.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.3 = "";
    $recipe_nama.3 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.3 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.3 = "";
    $recipe_qty.3 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.3 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.3 = "";
    
    $sb_3.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_3.status_resep = false;
    $sb_3.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_3.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_3.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_3.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_3 = 0;
    var activeSisa_3 = $sb_3.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_3 = $sb_3.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_3.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_3 = $sb_3.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_3 = activeSisa_3 + adjustSecs_3;
        if (activeSisa_3 < 0) {
            activeSisa_3 = 0;
        }
        $sb_3.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_3;
        
        activePerubahan_3 = activePerubahan_3 + $sb_3.adjust_menit;
        $sb_3.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_3;
        $sb_3.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb3._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_3.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_3.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_3.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_3.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_3.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb3._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_3.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_3 = ($sb3.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb3.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_3.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_3.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_3.mode_preheat || $sb_3.status_resep) {
                        $sb_3.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_3.mode_preheat && !$sb_3.status_resep && $sb_3.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_3 === 0 && !$sb_3.status_selesai && $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_3.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_3.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_3.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_3.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_3.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_3.status_kosong && !$sb_3.status_selesai && !$sb_3.mode_preheat && !$sb_3.status_resep) {
                        $sb_3.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_3.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_3.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_3.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_3.status_resep && activeSisa_3 === 0) {
                                $sb_3.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_3.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_3.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_3.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_3);
                        scale_up_3 = ((($sb_3.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_3) * 60) - activeSisa_3;
                        $sb_3.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_3 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_3);
                        if ($sb_3.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_3);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_3.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_3.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_3.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_3.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_3.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_3.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_3.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_3.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_3.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_3.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_3.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_3.suhu_awal = $sb3.temp;
                            activePerubahan_3 = 0;
                            $sb_3.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_3.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb3.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb3.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_3.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_3.suhu_akhir = $sb3.temp;
                            $sb_3.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_3.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_3.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_3.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_3.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_3.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_3.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_3 = $sb_3.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_3.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_3;
                            $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_3.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_3.suhu_awal = $sb3.temp;
                            activePerubahan_3 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_3.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb3.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_3.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_3.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_3.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_3.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_3.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_3);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_3 = ((($sb_3.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_3) * 60) - activeSisa_3) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_3;
                            $sb_3.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_3.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_3);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 3, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_3,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_3.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_3.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_3.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_3.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_3.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_3.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_3 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_3 = activeSisa_3 - 1;
                                $sb_3.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_3;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_3);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_3 = ((($sb_3.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_3) * 60) - activeSisa_3) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_3;
                            $sb_3.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_3 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_3 = 0;
                                $sb_3.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_3.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_3) * 60);
                                $sb_3.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb3.temp;
                                $sb_3.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb3.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_3.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_3.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_3.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 3;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.3;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.3;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.3;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.3;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.3;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.3;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.3;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_3.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_3.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_3.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_3.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_3; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_3.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_3.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_3);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 3, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_3,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_3.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_3.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_3) {
                    $sb_3.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb3.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_3.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_3.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_3.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_3.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_3.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_3.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_3.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_3.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_3.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_3.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_3.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 4
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_4.reset) {
    $sb_4.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_4.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_4.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_4.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_4.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_4.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_4.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_4.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_4.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_4.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_4.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_4.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.4 = "";
    $recipe_nama.4 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.4 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.4 = "";
    $recipe_qty.4 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.4 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.4 = "";
    
    $sb_4.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_4.status_resep = false;
    $sb_4.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_4.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_4.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_4.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_4 = 0;
    var activeSisa_4 = $sb_4.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_4 = $sb_4.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_4.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_4 = $sb_4.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_4 = activeSisa_4 + adjustSecs_4;
        if (activeSisa_4 < 0) {
            activeSisa_4 = 0;
        }
        $sb_4.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_4;
        
        activePerubahan_4 = activePerubahan_4 + $sb_4.adjust_menit;
        $sb_4.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_4;
        $sb_4.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb4._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_4.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_4.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_4.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_4.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_4.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb4._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_4.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_4 = ($sb4.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb4.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_4.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_4.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_4.mode_preheat || $sb_4.status_resep) {
                        $sb_4.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_4.mode_preheat && !$sb_4.status_resep && $sb_4.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_4 === 0 && !$sb_4.status_selesai && $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_4.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_4.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_4.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_4.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_4.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_4.status_kosong && !$sb_4.status_selesai && !$sb_4.mode_preheat && !$sb_4.status_resep) {
                        $sb_4.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_4.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_4.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_4.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_4.status_resep && activeSisa_4 === 0) {
                                $sb_4.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_4.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_4.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_4.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_4);
                        scale_up_4 = ((($sb_4.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_4) * 60) - activeSisa_4;
                        $sb_4.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_4 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_4);
                        if ($sb_4.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_4);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_4.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_4.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_4.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_4.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_4.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_4.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_4.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_4.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_4.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_4.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_4.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_4.suhu_awal = $sb4.temp;
                            activePerubahan_4 = 0;
                            $sb_4.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_4.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb4.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb4.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_4.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_4.suhu_akhir = $sb4.temp;
                            $sb_4.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_4.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_4.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_4.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_4.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_4.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_4.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_4 = $sb_4.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_4.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_4;
                            $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_4.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_4.suhu_awal = $sb4.temp;
                            activePerubahan_4 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_4.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb4.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_4.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_4.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_4.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_4.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_4.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_4);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_4 = ((($sb_4.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_4) * 60) - activeSisa_4) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_4;
                            $sb_4.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_4.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_4);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 4, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_4,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_4.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_4.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_4.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_4.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_4.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_4.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_4 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_4 = activeSisa_4 - 1;
                                $sb_4.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_4;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_4);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_4 = ((($sb_4.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_4) * 60) - activeSisa_4) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_4;
                            $sb_4.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_4 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_4 = 0;
                                $sb_4.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_4.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_4) * 60);
                                $sb_4.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb4.temp;
                                $sb_4.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb4.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_4.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_4.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_4.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 4;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.4;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.4;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.4;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.4;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.4;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.4;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.4;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_4.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_4.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_4.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_4.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_4; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_4.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_4.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_4);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 4, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_4,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_4.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_4.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_4) {
                    $sb_4.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb4.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_4.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_4.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_4.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_4.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_4.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_4.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_4.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_4.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_4.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_4.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_4.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 5
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_5.reset) {
    $sb_5.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_5.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_5.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_5.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_5.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_5.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_5.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_5.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_5.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_5.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_5.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_5.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.5 = "";
    $recipe_nama.5 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.5 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.5 = "";
    $recipe_qty.5 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.5 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.5 = "";
    
    $sb_5.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_5.status_resep = false;
    $sb_5.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_5.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_5.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_5.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_5 = 0;
    var activeSisa_5 = $sb_5.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_5 = $sb_5.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_5.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_5 = $sb_5.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_5 = activeSisa_5 + adjustSecs_5;
        if (activeSisa_5 < 0) {
            activeSisa_5 = 0;
        }
        $sb_5.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_5;
        
        activePerubahan_5 = activePerubahan_5 + $sb_5.adjust_menit;
        $sb_5.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_5;
        $sb_5.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb5._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_5.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_5.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_5.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_5.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_5.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb5._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_5.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_5 = ($sb5.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb5.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_5.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_5.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_5.mode_preheat || $sb_5.status_resep) {
                        $sb_5.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_5.mode_preheat && !$sb_5.status_resep && $sb_5.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_5 === 0 && !$sb_5.status_selesai && $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_5.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_5.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_5.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_5.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_5.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_5.status_kosong && !$sb_5.status_selesai && !$sb_5.mode_preheat && !$sb_5.status_resep) {
                        $sb_5.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_5.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_5.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_5.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_5.status_resep && activeSisa_5 === 0) {
                                $sb_5.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_5.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_5.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_5.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_5);
                        scale_up_5 = ((($sb_5.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_5) * 60) - activeSisa_5;
                        $sb_5.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_5 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_5);
                        if ($sb_5.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_5);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_5.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_5.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_5.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_5.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_5.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_5.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_5.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_5.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_5.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_5.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_5.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_5.suhu_awal = $sb5.temp;
                            activePerubahan_5 = 0;
                            $sb_5.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_5.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb5.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb5.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_5.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_5.suhu_akhir = $sb5.temp;
                            $sb_5.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_5.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_5.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_5.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_5.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_5.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_5.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_5 = $sb_5.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_5.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_5;
                            $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_5.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_5.suhu_awal = $sb5.temp;
                            activePerubahan_5 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_5.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb5.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_5.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_5.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_5.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_5.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_5.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_5);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_5 = ((($sb_5.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_5) * 60) - activeSisa_5) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_5;
                            $sb_5.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_5.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_5);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 5, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_5,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_5.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_5.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_5.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_5.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_5.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_5.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_5 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_5 = activeSisa_5 - 1;
                                $sb_5.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_5;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_5);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_5 = ((($sb_5.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_5) * 60) - activeSisa_5) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_5;
                            $sb_5.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_5 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_5 = 0;
                                $sb_5.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_5.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_5) * 60);
                                $sb_5.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb5.temp;
                                $sb_5.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb5.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_5.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_5.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_5.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 5;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.5;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.5;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.5;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.5;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.5;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.5;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.5;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_5.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_5.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_5.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_5.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_5; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_5.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_5.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_5);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 5, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_5,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_5.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_5.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_5) {
                    $sb_5.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb5.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_5.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_5.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_5.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
