                    $sb_5.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_5.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_5.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_5.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_5.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_5.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_5.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_5.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 6
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_6.reset) {
    $sb_6.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_6.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_6.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_6.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_6.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_6.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_6.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_6.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_6.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_6.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_6.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_6.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.6 = "";
    $recipe_nama.6 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.6 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.6 = "";
    $recipe_qty.6 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.6 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.6 = "";
    
    $sb_6.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_6.status_resep = false;
    $sb_6.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_6.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_6.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_6.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_6 = 0;
    var activeSisa_6 = $sb_6.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_6 = $sb_6.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_6.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_6 = $sb_6.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_6 = activeSisa_6 + adjustSecs_6;
        if (activeSisa_6 < 0) {
            activeSisa_6 = 0;
        }
        $sb_6.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_6;
        
        activePerubahan_6 = activePerubahan_6 + $sb_6.adjust_menit;
        $sb_6.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_6;
        $sb_6.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb6._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_6.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_6.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_6.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_6.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_6.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb6._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_6.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_6 = ($sb6.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb6.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_6.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_6.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_6.mode_preheat || $sb_6.status_resep) {
                        $sb_6.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_6.mode_preheat && !$sb_6.status_resep && $sb_6.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_6 === 0 && !$sb_6.status_selesai && $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_6.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_6.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_6.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_6.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_6.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_6.status_kosong && !$sb_6.status_selesai && !$sb_6.mode_preheat && !$sb_6.status_resep) {
                        $sb_6.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_6.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_6.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_6.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_6.status_resep && activeSisa_6 === 0) {
                                $sb_6.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_6.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_6.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_6.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_6);
                        scale_up_6 = ((($sb_6.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_6) * 60) - activeSisa_6;
                        $sb_6.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_6 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_6);
                        if ($sb_6.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_6);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_6.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_6.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_6.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_6.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_6.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_6.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_6.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_6.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_6.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_6.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_6.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_6.suhu_awal = $sb6.temp;
                            activePerubahan_6 = 0;
                            $sb_6.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_6.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb6.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb6.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_6.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_6.suhu_akhir = $sb6.temp;
                            $sb_6.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_6.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_6.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_6.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_6.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_6.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_6.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_6 = $sb_6.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_6.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_6;
                            $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_6.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_6.suhu_awal = $sb6.temp;
                            activePerubahan_6 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_6.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb6.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_6.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_6.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_6.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_6.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_6.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_6);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_6 = ((($sb_6.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_6) * 60) - activeSisa_6) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_6;
                            $sb_6.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_6.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_6);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 6, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_6,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_6.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_6.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_6.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_6.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_6.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_6.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_6 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_6 = activeSisa_6 - 1;
                                $sb_6.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_6;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_6);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_6 = ((($sb_6.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_6) * 60) - activeSisa_6) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_6;
                            $sb_6.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_6 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_6 = 0;
                                $sb_6.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_6.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_6) * 60);
                                $sb_6.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb6.temp;
                                $sb_6.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb6.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_6.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_6.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_6.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 6;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.6;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.6;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.6;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.6;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.6;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.6;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.6;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_6.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_6.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_6.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_6.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_6; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_6.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_6.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_6);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 6, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_6,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_6.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_6.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_6) {
                    $sb_6.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb6.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_6.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_6.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_6.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_6.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_6.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_6.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_6.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_6.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_6.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_6.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_6.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 7
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_7.reset) {
    $sb_7.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_7.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_7.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_7.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_7.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_7.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_7.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_7.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_7.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_7.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_7.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_7.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.7 = "";
    $recipe_nama.7 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.7 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.7 = "";
    $recipe_qty.7 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.7 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.7 = "";
    
    $sb_7.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_7.status_resep = false;
    $sb_7.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_7.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_7.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_7.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_7 = 0;
    var activeSisa_7 = $sb_7.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_7 = $sb_7.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_7.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_7 = $sb_7.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_7 = activeSisa_7 + adjustSecs_7;
        if (activeSisa_7 < 0) {
            activeSisa_7 = 0;
        }
        $sb_7.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_7;
        
        activePerubahan_7 = activePerubahan_7 + $sb_7.adjust_menit;
        $sb_7.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_7;
        $sb_7.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb7._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_7.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_7.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_7.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_7.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_7.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb7._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_7.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_7 = ($sb7.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb7.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_7.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_7.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_7.mode_preheat || $sb_7.status_resep) {
                        $sb_7.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_7.mode_preheat && !$sb_7.status_resep && $sb_7.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_7 === 0 && !$sb_7.status_selesai && $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_7.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_7.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_7.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_7.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_7.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_7.status_kosong && !$sb_7.status_selesai && !$sb_7.mode_preheat && !$sb_7.status_resep) {
                        $sb_7.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_7.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_7.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_7.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_7.status_resep && activeSisa_7 === 0) {
                                $sb_7.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_7.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_7.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_7.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_7);
                        scale_up_7 = ((($sb_7.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_7) * 60) - activeSisa_7;
                        $sb_7.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_7 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_7);
                        if ($sb_7.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_7);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_7.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_7.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_7.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_7.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_7.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_7.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_7.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_7.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_7.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_7.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_7.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_7.suhu_awal = $sb7.temp;
                            activePerubahan_7 = 0;
                            $sb_7.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_7.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb7.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb7.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_7.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_7.suhu_akhir = $sb7.temp;
                            $sb_7.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_7.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_7.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_7.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_7.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_7.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_7.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_7 = $sb_7.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_7.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_7;
                            $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_7.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_7.suhu_awal = $sb7.temp;
                            activePerubahan_7 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_7.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb7.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_7.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_7.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_7.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_7.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_7.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_7);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_7 = ((($sb_7.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_7) * 60) - activeSisa_7) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_7;
                            $sb_7.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_7.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_7);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 7, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_7,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_7.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_7.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_7.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_7.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_7.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_7.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_7 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_7 = activeSisa_7 - 1;
                                $sb_7.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_7;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_7);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_7 = ((($sb_7.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_7) * 60) - activeSisa_7) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_7;
                            $sb_7.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_7 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_7 = 0;
                                $sb_7.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_7.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_7) * 60);
                                $sb_7.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb7.temp;
                                $sb_7.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb7.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_7.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_7.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_7.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 7;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.7;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.7;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.7;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.7;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.7;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.7;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.7;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_7.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_7.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_7.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_7.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_7; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_7.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_7.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_7);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 7, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_7,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_7.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_7.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_7) {
                    $sb_7.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb7.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_7.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_7.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_7.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_7.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_7.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_7.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_7.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_7.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_7.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_7.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_7.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 8
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_8.reset) {
    $sb_8.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_8.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_8.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_8.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_8.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_8.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_8.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_8.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_8.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_8.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_8.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_8.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.8 = "";
    $recipe_nama.8 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.8 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.8 = "";
    $recipe_qty.8 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.8 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.8 = "";
    
    $sb_8.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_8.status_resep = false;
    $sb_8.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_8.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_8.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_8.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_8 = 0;
    var activeSisa_8 = $sb_8.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_8 = $sb_8.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_8.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_8 = $sb_8.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_8 = activeSisa_8 + adjustSecs_8;
        if (activeSisa_8 < 0) {
            activeSisa_8 = 0;
        }
        $sb_8.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_8;
        
        activePerubahan_8 = activePerubahan_8 + $sb_8.adjust_menit;
        $sb_8.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_8;
        $sb_8.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb8._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_8.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_8.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_8.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_8.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_8.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb8._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_8.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_8 = ($sb8.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb8.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_8.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_8.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_8.mode_preheat || $sb_8.status_resep) {
                        $sb_8.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_8.mode_preheat && !$sb_8.status_resep && $sb_8.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_8 === 0 && !$sb_8.status_selesai && $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_8.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_8.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_8.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_8.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_8.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_8.status_kosong && !$sb_8.status_selesai && !$sb_8.mode_preheat && !$sb_8.status_resep) {
                        $sb_8.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_8.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_8.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_8.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_8.status_resep && activeSisa_8 === 0) {
                                $sb_8.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_8.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_8.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_8.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_8);
                        scale_up_8 = ((($sb_8.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_8) * 60) - activeSisa_8;
                        $sb_8.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_8 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_8);
                        if ($sb_8.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_8);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_8.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_8.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_8.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_8.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_8.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_8.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_8.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_8.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_8.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_8.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_8.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_8.suhu_awal = $sb8.temp;
                            activePerubahan_8 = 0;
                            $sb_8.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_8.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb8.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb8.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_8.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_8.suhu_akhir = $sb8.temp;
                            $sb_8.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_8.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_8.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_8.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_8.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_8.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_8.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_8 = $sb_8.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_8.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_8;
                            $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_8.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_8.suhu_awal = $sb8.temp;
                            activePerubahan_8 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_8.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb8.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_8.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_8.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_8.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_8.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_8.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_8);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_8 = ((($sb_8.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_8) * 60) - activeSisa_8) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_8;
                            $sb_8.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_8.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_8);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 8, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_8,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_8.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_8.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_8.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_8.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_8.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_8.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_8 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_8 = activeSisa_8 - 1;
                                $sb_8.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_8;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_8);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_8 = ((($sb_8.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_8) * 60) - activeSisa_8) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_8;
                            $sb_8.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_8 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_8 = 0;
                                $sb_8.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_8.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_8) * 60);
                                $sb_8.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb8.temp;
                                $sb_8.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb8.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_8.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_8.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_8.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 8;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.8;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.8;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.8;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.8;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.8;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.8;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.8;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_8.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_8.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_8.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_8.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_8; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_8.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_8.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_8);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 8, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_8,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_8.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_8.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_8) {
                    $sb_8.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb8.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_8.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_8.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_8.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_8.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_8.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_8.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_8.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_8.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_8.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_8.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_8.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 9
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_9.reset) {
    $sb_9.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_9.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_9.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_9.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_9.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_9.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_9.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_9.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_9.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_9.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_9.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_9.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.9 = "";
    $recipe_nama.9 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.9 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.9 = "";
    $recipe_qty.9 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.9 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.9 = "";
    
    $sb_9.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_9.status_resep = false;
    $sb_9.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_9.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_9.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_9.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_9 = 0;
    var activeSisa_9 = $sb_9.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_9 = $sb_9.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_9.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_9 = $sb_9.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_9 = activeSisa_9 + adjustSecs_9;
        if (activeSisa_9 < 0) {
            activeSisa_9 = 0;
        }
        $sb_9.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_9;
        
        activePerubahan_9 = activePerubahan_9 + $sb_9.adjust_menit;
        $sb_9.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_9;
        $sb_9.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb9._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_9.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_9.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_9.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_9.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_9.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb9._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_9.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_9 = ($sb9.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb9.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_9.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_9.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_9.mode_preheat || $sb_9.status_resep) {
                        $sb_9.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_9.mode_preheat && !$sb_9.status_resep && $sb_9.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_9 === 0 && !$sb_9.status_selesai && $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_9.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_9.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_9.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_9.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_9.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_9.status_kosong && !$sb_9.status_selesai && !$sb_9.mode_preheat && !$sb_9.status_resep) {
                        $sb_9.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_9.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_9.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_9.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_9.status_resep && activeSisa_9 === 0) {
                                $sb_9.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_9.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_9.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_9.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_9);
                        scale_up_9 = ((($sb_9.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_9) * 60) - activeSisa_9;
                        $sb_9.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_9 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_9);
                        if ($sb_9.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_9);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_9.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_9.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_9.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_9.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_9.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_9.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_9.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_9.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_9.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_9.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_9.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_9.suhu_awal = $sb9.temp;
                            activePerubahan_9 = 0;
                            $sb_9.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_9.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb9.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb9.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_9.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_9.suhu_akhir = $sb9.temp;
                            $sb_9.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_9.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_9.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_9.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_9.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_9.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_9.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_9 = $sb_9.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_9.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_9;
                            $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_9.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_9.suhu_awal = $sb9.temp;
                            activePerubahan_9 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_9.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb9.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_9.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_9.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_9.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_9.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_9.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_9);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_9 = ((($sb_9.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_9) * 60) - activeSisa_9) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_9;
                            $sb_9.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_9.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_9);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 9, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_9,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_9.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_9.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_9.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_9.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_9.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_9.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_9 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_9 = activeSisa_9 - 1;
                                $sb_9.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_9;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_9);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_9 = ((($sb_9.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_9) * 60) - activeSisa_9) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_9;
                            $sb_9.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_9 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_9 = 0;
                                $sb_9.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_9.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_9) * 60);
                                $sb_9.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb9.temp;
                                $sb_9.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb9.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_9.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_9.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_9.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 9;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.9;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.9;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.9;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.9;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.9;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.9;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.9;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_9.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_9.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_9.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_9.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_9; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_9.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_9.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_9);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 9, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_9,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_9.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_9.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_9) {
                    $sb_9.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb9.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_9.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_9.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_9.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_9.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_9.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_9.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_9.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_9.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_9.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_9.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_9.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 10
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_10.reset) {
    $sb_10.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_10.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_10.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_10.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_10.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_10.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_10.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_10.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_10.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_10.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_10.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_10.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.10 = "";
    $recipe_nama.10 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.10 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.10 = "";
    $recipe_qty.10 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.10 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.10 = "";
    
    $sb_10.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_10.status_resep = false;
    $sb_10.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_10.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_10.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_10.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_10 = 0;
    var activeSisa_10 = $sb_10.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_10 = $sb_10.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_10.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_10 = $sb_10.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_10 = activeSisa_10 + adjustSecs_10;
        if (activeSisa_10 < 0) {
            activeSisa_10 = 0;
        }
        $sb_10.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_10;
        
        activePerubahan_10 = activePerubahan_10 + $sb_10.adjust_menit;
        $sb_10.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_10;
        $sb_10.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb10._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_10.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_10.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_10.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_10.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_10.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb10._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_10.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_10 = ($sb10.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb10.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_10.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_10.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_10.mode_preheat || $sb_10.status_resep) {
                        $sb_10.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_10.mode_preheat && !$sb_10.status_resep && $sb_10.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_10 === 0 && !$sb_10.status_selesai && $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_10.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_10.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_10.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_10.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_10.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_10.status_kosong && !$sb_10.status_selesai && !$sb_10.mode_preheat && !$sb_10.status_resep) {
                        $sb_10.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_10.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_10.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_10.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_10.status_resep && activeSisa_10 === 0) {
                                $sb_10.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_10.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_10.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_10.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_10);
                        scale_up_10 = ((($sb_10.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_10) * 60) - activeSisa_10;
                        $sb_10.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_10 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_10);
                        if ($sb_10.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_10);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_10.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_10.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_10.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_10.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_10.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_10.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_10.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_10.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_10.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_10.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_10.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_10.suhu_awal = $sb10.temp;
                            activePerubahan_10 = 0;
                            $sb_10.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_10.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb10.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb10.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_10.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_10.suhu_akhir = $sb10.temp;
                            $sb_10.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_10.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_10.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_10.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_10.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_10.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_10.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_10 = $sb_10.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_10.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_10;
                            $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_10.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_10.suhu_awal = $sb10.temp;
                            activePerubahan_10 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_10.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb10.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_10.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_10.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_10.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_10.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_10.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_10);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_10 = ((($sb_10.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_10) * 60) - activeSisa_10) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_10;
                            $sb_10.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_10.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_10);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 10, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_10,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_10.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_10.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_10.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_10.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_10.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_10.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_10 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_10 = activeSisa_10 - 1;
                                $sb_10.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_10;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_10);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_10 = ((($sb_10.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_10) * 60) - activeSisa_10) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_10;
                            $sb_10.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_10 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_10 = 0;
                                $sb_10.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_10.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_10) * 60);
                                $sb_10.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb10.temp;
                                $sb_10.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb10.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_10.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_10.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_10.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 10;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.10;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.10;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.10;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.10;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.10;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.10;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.10;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_10.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_10.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_10.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_10.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_10; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_10.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_10.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_10);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 10, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_10,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_10.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_10.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_10) {
                    $sb_10.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb10.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_10.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_10.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_10.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_10.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_10.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_10.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_10.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_10.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_10.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_10.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_10.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 11
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_11.reset) {
    $sb_11.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_11.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_11.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_11.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_11.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_11.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_11.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_11.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_11.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_11.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_11.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_11.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.11 = "";
    $recipe_nama.11 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.11 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.11 = "";
    $recipe_qty.11 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.11 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.11 = "";
    
    $sb_11.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_11.status_resep = false;
    $sb_11.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_11.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_11.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_11.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_11 = 0;
    var activeSisa_11 = $sb_11.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_11 = $sb_11.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_11.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_11 = $sb_11.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_11 = activeSisa_11 + adjustSecs_11;
        if (activeSisa_11 < 0) {
            activeSisa_11 = 0;
        }
        $sb_11.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_11;
        
        activePerubahan_11 = activePerubahan_11 + $sb_11.adjust_menit;
        $sb_11.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_11;
        $sb_11.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb11._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_11.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_11.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_11.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_11.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_11.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb11._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_11.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_11 = ($sb11.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb11.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_11.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_11.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_11.mode_preheat || $sb_11.status_resep) {
                        $sb_11.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
