                    if (!$sb_11.mode_preheat && !$sb_11.status_resep && $sb_11.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_11 === 0 && !$sb_11.status_selesai && $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_11.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_11.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_11.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_11.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_11.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_11.status_kosong && !$sb_11.status_selesai && !$sb_11.mode_preheat && !$sb_11.status_resep) {
                        $sb_11.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_11.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_11.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_11.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_11.status_resep && activeSisa_11 === 0) {
                                $sb_11.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_11.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_11.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_11.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_11);
                        scale_up_11 = ((($sb_11.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_11) * 60) - activeSisa_11;
                        $sb_11.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_11 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_11);
                        if ($sb_11.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_11);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_11.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_11.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_11.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_11.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_11.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_11.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_11.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_11.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_11.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_11.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_11.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_11.suhu_awal = $sb11.temp;
                            activePerubahan_11 = 0;
                            $sb_11.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_11.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb11.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb11.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_11.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_11.suhu_akhir = $sb11.temp;
                            $sb_11.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_11.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_11.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_11.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_11.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_11.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_11.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_11 = $sb_11.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_11.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_11;
                            $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_11.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_11.suhu_awal = $sb11.temp;
                            activePerubahan_11 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_11.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb11.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_11.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_11.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_11.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_11.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_11.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_11);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_11 = ((($sb_11.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_11) * 60) - activeSisa_11) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_11;
                            $sb_11.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_11.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_11);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 11, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_11,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_11.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_11.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_11.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_11.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_11.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_11.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_11 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_11 = activeSisa_11 - 1;
                                $sb_11.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_11;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_11);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_11 = ((($sb_11.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_11) * 60) - activeSisa_11) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_11;
                            $sb_11.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_11 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_11 = 0;
                                $sb_11.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_11.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_11) * 60);
                                $sb_11.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb11.temp;
                                $sb_11.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb11.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_11.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_11.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_11.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 11;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.11;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.11;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.11;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.11;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.11;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.11;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.11;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_11.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_11.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_11.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_11.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_11; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_11.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_11.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_11);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 11, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_11,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_11.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_11.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_11) {
                    $sb_11.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb11.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_11.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_11.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_11.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_11.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_11.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_11.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_11.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_11.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_11.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_11.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_11.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 12
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_12.reset) {
    $sb_12.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_12.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_12.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_12.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_12.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_12.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_12.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_12.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_12.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_12.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_12.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_12.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.12 = "";
    $recipe_nama.12 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.12 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.12 = "";
    $recipe_qty.12 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.12 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.12 = "";
    
    $sb_12.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_12.status_resep = false;
    $sb_12.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_12.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_12.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_12.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_12 = 0;
    var activeSisa_12 = $sb_12.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_12 = $sb_12.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_12.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_12 = $sb_12.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_12 = activeSisa_12 + adjustSecs_12;
        if (activeSisa_12 < 0) {
            activeSisa_12 = 0;
        }
        $sb_12.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_12;
        
        activePerubahan_12 = activePerubahan_12 + $sb_12.adjust_menit;
        $sb_12.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_12;
        $sb_12.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb12._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_12.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_12.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_12.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_12.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_12.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb12._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_12.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_12 = ($sb12.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb12.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_12.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_12.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_12.mode_preheat || $sb_12.status_resep) {
                        $sb_12.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_12.mode_preheat && !$sb_12.status_resep && $sb_12.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_12 === 0 && !$sb_12.status_selesai && $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_12.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_12.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_12.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_12.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_12.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_12.status_kosong && !$sb_12.status_selesai && !$sb_12.mode_preheat && !$sb_12.status_resep) {
                        $sb_12.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_12.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_12.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_12.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_12.status_resep && activeSisa_12 === 0) {
                                $sb_12.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_12.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_12.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_12.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_12);
                        scale_up_12 = ((($sb_12.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_12) * 60) - activeSisa_12;
                        $sb_12.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_12 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_12);
                        if ($sb_12.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_12);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_12.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_12.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_12.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_12.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_12.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_12.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_12.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_12.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_12.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_12.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_12.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_12.suhu_awal = $sb12.temp;
                            activePerubahan_12 = 0;
                            $sb_12.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_12.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb12.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb12.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_12.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_12.suhu_akhir = $sb12.temp;
                            $sb_12.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_12.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_12.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_12.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_12.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_12.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_12.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_12 = $sb_12.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_12.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_12;
                            $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_12.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_12.suhu_awal = $sb12.temp;
                            activePerubahan_12 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_12.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb12.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_12.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_12.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_12.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_12.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_12.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_12);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_12 = ((($sb_12.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_12) * 60) - activeSisa_12) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_12;
                            $sb_12.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_12.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_12);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 12, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_12,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_12.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_12.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_12.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_12.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_12.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_12.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_12 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_12 = activeSisa_12 - 1;
                                $sb_12.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_12;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_12);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_12 = ((($sb_12.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_12) * 60) - activeSisa_12) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_12;
                            $sb_12.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_12 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_12 = 0;
                                $sb_12.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_12.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_12) * 60);
                                $sb_12.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb12.temp;
                                $sb_12.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb12.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_12.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_12.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_12.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 12;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.12;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.12;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.12;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.12;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.12;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.12;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.12;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_12.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_12.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_12.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_12.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_12; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_12.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_12.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_12);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 12, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_12,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_12.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_12.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_12) {
                    $sb_12.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb12.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_12.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_12.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_12.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_12.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_12.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_12.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_12.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_12.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_12.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_12.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_12.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 13
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_13.reset) {
    $sb_13.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_13.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_13.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_13.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_13.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_13.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_13.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_13.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_13.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_13.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_13.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_13.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.13 = "";
    $recipe_nama.13 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.13 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.13 = "";
    $recipe_qty.13 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.13 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.13 = "";
    
    $sb_13.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_13.status_resep = false;
    $sb_13.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_13.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_13.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_13.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_13 = 0;
    var activeSisa_13 = $sb_13.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_13 = $sb_13.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_13.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_13 = $sb_13.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_13 = activeSisa_13 + adjustSecs_13;
        if (activeSisa_13 < 0) {
            activeSisa_13 = 0;
        }
        $sb_13.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_13;
        
        activePerubahan_13 = activePerubahan_13 + $sb_13.adjust_menit;
        $sb_13.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_13;
        $sb_13.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb13._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_13.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_13.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_13.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_13.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_13.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb13._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_13.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_13 = ($sb13.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb13.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_13.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_13.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_13.mode_preheat || $sb_13.status_resep) {
                        $sb_13.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_13.mode_preheat && !$sb_13.status_resep && $sb_13.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_13 === 0 && !$sb_13.status_selesai && $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_13.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_13.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_13.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_13.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_13.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_13.status_kosong && !$sb_13.status_selesai && !$sb_13.mode_preheat && !$sb_13.status_resep) {
                        $sb_13.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_13.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_13.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_13.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_13.status_resep && activeSisa_13 === 0) {
                                $sb_13.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_13.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_13.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_13.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_13);
                        scale_up_13 = ((($sb_13.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_13) * 60) - activeSisa_13;
                        $sb_13.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_13 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_13);
                        if ($sb_13.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_13);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_13.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_13.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_13.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_13.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_13.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_13.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_13.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_13.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_13.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_13.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_13.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_13.suhu_awal = $sb13.temp;
                            activePerubahan_13 = 0;
                            $sb_13.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_13.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb13.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb13.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_13.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_13.suhu_akhir = $sb13.temp;
                            $sb_13.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_13.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_13.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_13.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_13.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_13.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_13.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_13 = $sb_13.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_13.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_13;
                            $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_13.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_13.suhu_awal = $sb13.temp;
                            activePerubahan_13 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_13.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb13.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_13.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_13.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_13.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_13.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_13.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_13);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_13 = ((($sb_13.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_13) * 60) - activeSisa_13) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_13;
                            $sb_13.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_13.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_13);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 13, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_13,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_13.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_13.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_13.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_13.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_13.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_13.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_13 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_13 = activeSisa_13 - 1;
                                $sb_13.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_13;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_13);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_13 = ((($sb_13.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_13) * 60) - activeSisa_13) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_13;
                            $sb_13.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_13 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_13 = 0;
                                $sb_13.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_13.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_13) * 60);
                                $sb_13.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb13.temp;
                                $sb_13.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb13.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_13.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_13.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_13.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 13;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.13;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.13;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.13;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.13;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.13;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.13;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.13;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_13.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_13.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_13.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_13.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_13; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_13.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_13.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_13);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 13, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_13,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_13.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_13.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_13) {
                    $sb_13.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb13.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_13.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_13.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_13.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_13.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_13.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_13.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_13.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_13.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_13.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_13.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_13.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 14
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_14.reset) {
    $sb_14.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_14.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_14.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_14.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_14.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_14.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_14.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_14.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_14.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_14.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_14.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_14.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.14 = "";
    $recipe_nama.14 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.14 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.14 = "";
    $recipe_qty.14 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.14 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.14 = "";
    
    $sb_14.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_14.status_resep = false;
    $sb_14.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_14.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_14.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_14.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_14 = 0;
    var activeSisa_14 = $sb_14.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_14 = $sb_14.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_14.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_14 = $sb_14.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_14 = activeSisa_14 + adjustSecs_14;
        if (activeSisa_14 < 0) {
            activeSisa_14 = 0;
        }
        $sb_14.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_14;
        
        activePerubahan_14 = activePerubahan_14 + $sb_14.adjust_menit;
        $sb_14.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_14;
        $sb_14.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb14._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_14.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_14.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_14.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_14.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_14.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb14._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_14.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_14 = ($sb14.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb14.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_14.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_14.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_14.mode_preheat || $sb_14.status_resep) {
                        $sb_14.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_14.mode_preheat && !$sb_14.status_resep && $sb_14.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_14 === 0 && !$sb_14.status_selesai && $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_14.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_14.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_14.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_14.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_14.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_14.status_kosong && !$sb_14.status_selesai && !$sb_14.mode_preheat && !$sb_14.status_resep) {
                        $sb_14.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_14.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_14.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_14.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_14.status_resep && activeSisa_14 === 0) {
                                $sb_14.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_14.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_14.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_14.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_14);
                        scale_up_14 = ((($sb_14.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_14) * 60) - activeSisa_14;
                        $sb_14.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_14 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_14);
                        if ($sb_14.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_14);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_14.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_14.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_14.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_14.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_14.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_14.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_14.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_14.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_14.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_14.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_14.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_14.suhu_awal = $sb14.temp;
                            activePerubahan_14 = 0;
                            $sb_14.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_14.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb14.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb14.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_14.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_14.suhu_akhir = $sb14.temp;
                            $sb_14.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_14.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_14.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_14.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_14.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_14.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_14.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_14 = $sb_14.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_14.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_14;
                            $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_14.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_14.suhu_awal = $sb14.temp;
                            activePerubahan_14 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_14.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb14.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_14.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_14.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_14.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_14.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_14.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_14);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_14 = ((($sb_14.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_14) * 60) - activeSisa_14) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_14;
                            $sb_14.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_14.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_14);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 14, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_14,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_14.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_14.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_14.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_14.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_14.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_14.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_14 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_14 = activeSisa_14 - 1;
                                $sb_14.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_14;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_14);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_14 = ((($sb_14.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_14) * 60) - activeSisa_14) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_14;
                            $sb_14.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_14 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_14 = 0;
                                $sb_14.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_14.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_14) * 60);
                                $sb_14.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb14.temp;
                                $sb_14.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb14.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_14.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_14.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_14.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 14;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.14;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.14;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.14;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.14;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.14;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.14;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.14;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_14.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_14.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_14.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_14.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_14; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_14.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_14.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_14);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 14, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_14,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_14.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_14.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_14) {
                    $sb_14.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb14.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_14.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_14.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_14.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_14.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_14.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_14.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_14.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_14.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_14.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_14.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_14.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 15
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_15.reset) {
    $sb_15.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_15.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_15.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_15.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_15.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_15.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_15.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_15.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_15.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_15.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_15.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_15.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.15 = "";
    $recipe_nama.15 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.15 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.15 = "";
    $recipe_qty.15 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.15 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.15 = "";
    
    $sb_15.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_15.status_resep = false;
    $sb_15.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_15.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_15.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_15.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_15 = 0;
    var activeSisa_15 = $sb_15.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_15 = $sb_15.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_15.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_15 = $sb_15.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_15 = activeSisa_15 + adjustSecs_15;
        if (activeSisa_15 < 0) {
            activeSisa_15 = 0;
        }
        $sb_15.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_15;
        
        activePerubahan_15 = activePerubahan_15 + $sb_15.adjust_menit;
        $sb_15.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_15;
        $sb_15.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb15._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_15.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_15.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_15.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_15.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_15.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb15._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_15.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_15 = ($sb15.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb15.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_15.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_15.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_15.mode_preheat || $sb_15.status_resep) {
                        $sb_15.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_15.mode_preheat && !$sb_15.status_resep && $sb_15.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_15 === 0 && !$sb_15.status_selesai && $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_15.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_15.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_15.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_15.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_15.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_15.status_kosong && !$sb_15.status_selesai && !$sb_15.mode_preheat && !$sb_15.status_resep) {
                        $sb_15.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_15.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_15.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_15.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_15.status_resep && activeSisa_15 === 0) {
                                $sb_15.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_15.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_15.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_15.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_15);
                        scale_up_15 = ((($sb_15.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_15) * 60) - activeSisa_15;
                        $sb_15.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_15 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_15);
                        if ($sb_15.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_15);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_15.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_15.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_15.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_15.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_15.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_15.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_15.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_15.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_15.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_15.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_15.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_15.suhu_awal = $sb15.temp;
                            activePerubahan_15 = 0;
                            $sb_15.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_15.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb15.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb15.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_15.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_15.suhu_akhir = $sb15.temp;
                            $sb_15.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_15.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_15.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_15.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_15.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_15.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_15.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_15 = $sb_15.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_15.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_15;
                            $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_15.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_15.suhu_awal = $sb15.temp;
                            activePerubahan_15 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_15.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb15.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_15.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_15.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_15.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_15.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_15.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_15);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_15 = ((($sb_15.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_15) * 60) - activeSisa_15) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_15;
                            $sb_15.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_15.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_15);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 15, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_15,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_15.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_15.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_15.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_15.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_15.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_15.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_15 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_15 = activeSisa_15 - 1;
                                $sb_15.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_15;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_15);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_15 = ((($sb_15.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_15) * 60) - activeSisa_15) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_15;
                            $sb_15.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_15 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_15 = 0;
                                $sb_15.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_15.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_15) * 60);
                                $sb_15.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb15.temp;
                                $sb_15.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb15.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_15.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_15.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_15.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 15;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.15;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.15;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.15;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.15;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.15;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.15;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.15;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_15.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_15.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_15.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_15.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_15; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_15.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_15.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_15);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 15, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_15,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_15.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_15.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_15) {
                    $sb_15.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb15.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_15.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_15.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_15.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_15.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_15.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_15.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_15.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_15.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_15.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_15.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_15.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 16
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_16.reset) {
    $sb_16.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_16.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_16.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_16.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_16.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_16.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_16.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_16.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_16.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_16.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_16.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_16.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.16 = "";
    $recipe_nama.16 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.16 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.16 = "";
    $recipe_qty.16 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.16 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.16 = "";
    
    $sb_16.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_16.status_resep = false;
    $sb_16.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_16.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_16.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_16.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_16 = 0;
    var activeSisa_16 = $sb_16.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_16 = $sb_16.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_16.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_16 = $sb_16.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_16 = activeSisa_16 + adjustSecs_16;
        if (activeSisa_16 < 0) {
            activeSisa_16 = 0;
        }
        $sb_16.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_16;
        
        activePerubahan_16 = activePerubahan_16 + $sb_16.adjust_menit;
        $sb_16.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_16;
        $sb_16.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb16._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_16.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_16.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_16.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_16.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_16.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb16._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_16.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_16 = ($sb16.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb16.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_16.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_16.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_16.mode_preheat || $sb_16.status_resep) {
                        $sb_16.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_16.mode_preheat && !$sb_16.status_resep && $sb_16.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_16 === 0 && !$sb_16.status_selesai && $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_16.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_16.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_16.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_16.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_16.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_16.status_kosong && !$sb_16.status_selesai && !$sb_16.mode_preheat && !$sb_16.status_resep) {
                        $sb_16.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_16.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_16.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_16.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_16.status_resep && activeSisa_16 === 0) {
                                $sb_16.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_16.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_16.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_16.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_16);
                        scale_up_16 = ((($sb_16.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_16) * 60) - activeSisa_16;
                        $sb_16.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_16 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_16);
                        if ($sb_16.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_16);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_16.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_16.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
