                        $sb_16.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_16.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_16.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_16.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_16.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_16.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_16.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_16.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_16.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_16.suhu_awal = $sb16.temp;
                            activePerubahan_16 = 0;
                            $sb_16.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_16.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb16.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb16.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_16.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_16.suhu_akhir = $sb16.temp;
                            $sb_16.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_16.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_16.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_16.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_16.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_16.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_16.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_16 = $sb_16.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_16.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_16;
                            $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_16.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_16.suhu_awal = $sb16.temp;
                            activePerubahan_16 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_16.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb16.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_16.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_16.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_16.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_16.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_16.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_16);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_16 = ((($sb_16.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_16) * 60) - activeSisa_16) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_16;
                            $sb_16.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_16.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_16);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 16, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_16,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_16.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_16.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_16.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_16.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_16.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_16.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_16 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_16 = activeSisa_16 - 1;
                                $sb_16.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_16;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_16);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_16 = ((($sb_16.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_16) * 60) - activeSisa_16) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_16;
                            $sb_16.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_16 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_16 = 0;
                                $sb_16.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_16.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_16) * 60);
                                $sb_16.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb16.temp;
                                $sb_16.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb16.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_16.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_16.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_16.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 16;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.16;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.16;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.16;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.16;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.16;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.16;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.16;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_16.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_16.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_16.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_16.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_16; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_16.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_16.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_16);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 16, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_16,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_16.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_16.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_16) {
                    $sb_16.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb16.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_16.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_16.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_16.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_16.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_16.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_16.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_16.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_16.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_16.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_16.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_16.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 17
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_17.reset) {
    $sb_17.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_17.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_17.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_17.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_17.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_17.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_17.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_17.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_17.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_17.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_17.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_17.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.17 = "";
    $recipe_nama.17 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.17 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.17 = "";
    $recipe_qty.17 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.17 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.17 = "";
    
    $sb_17.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_17.status_resep = false;
    $sb_17.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_17.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_17.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_17.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_17 = 0;
    var activeSisa_17 = $sb_17.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_17 = $sb_17.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_17.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_17 = $sb_17.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_17 = activeSisa_17 + adjustSecs_17;
        if (activeSisa_17 < 0) {
            activeSisa_17 = 0;
        }
        $sb_17.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_17;
        
        activePerubahan_17 = activePerubahan_17 + $sb_17.adjust_menit;
        $sb_17.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_17;
        $sb_17.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb17._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_17.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_17.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_17.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_17.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_17.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb17._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_17.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_17 = ($sb17.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb17.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_17.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_17.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_17.mode_preheat || $sb_17.status_resep) {
                        $sb_17.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_17.mode_preheat && !$sb_17.status_resep && $sb_17.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_17 === 0 && !$sb_17.status_selesai && $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_17.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_17.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_17.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_17.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_17.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_17.status_kosong && !$sb_17.status_selesai && !$sb_17.mode_preheat && !$sb_17.status_resep) {
                        $sb_17.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_17.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_17.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_17.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_17.status_resep && activeSisa_17 === 0) {
                                $sb_17.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_17.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_17.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_17.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_17);
                        scale_up_17 = ((($sb_17.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_17) * 60) - activeSisa_17;
                        $sb_17.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_17 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_17);
                        if ($sb_17.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_17);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_17.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_17.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_17.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_17.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_17.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_17.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_17.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_17.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_17.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_17.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_17.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_17.suhu_awal = $sb17.temp;
                            activePerubahan_17 = 0;
                            $sb_17.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_17.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb17.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb17.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_17.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_17.suhu_akhir = $sb17.temp;
                            $sb_17.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_17.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_17.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_17.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_17.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_17.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_17.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_17 = $sb_17.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_17.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_17;
                            $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_17.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_17.suhu_awal = $sb17.temp;
                            activePerubahan_17 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_17.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb17.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_17.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_17.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_17.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_17.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_17.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_17);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_17 = ((($sb_17.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_17) * 60) - activeSisa_17) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_17;
                            $sb_17.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_17.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_17);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 17, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_17,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_17.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_17.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_17.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_17.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_17.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_17.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_17 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_17 = activeSisa_17 - 1;
                                $sb_17.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_17;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_17);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_17 = ((($sb_17.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_17) * 60) - activeSisa_17) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_17;
                            $sb_17.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_17 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_17 = 0;
                                $sb_17.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_17.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_17) * 60);
                                $sb_17.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb17.temp;
                                $sb_17.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb17.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_17.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_17.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_17.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 17;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.17;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.17;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.17;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.17;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.17;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.17;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.17;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_17.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_17.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_17.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_17.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_17; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_17.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_17.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_17);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 17, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_17,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_17.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_17.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_17) {
                    $sb_17.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb17.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_17.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_17.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_17.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_17.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_17.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_17.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_17.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_17.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_17.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_17.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_17.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 18
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_18.reset) {
    $sb_18.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_18.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_18.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_18.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_18.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_18.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_18.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_18.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_18.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_18.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_18.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_18.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.18 = "";
    $recipe_nama.18 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.18 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.18 = "";
    $recipe_qty.18 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.18 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.18 = "";
    
    $sb_18.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_18.status_resep = false;
    $sb_18.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_18.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_18.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_18.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_18 = 0;
    var activeSisa_18 = $sb_18.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_18 = $sb_18.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_18.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_18 = $sb_18.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_18 = activeSisa_18 + adjustSecs_18;
        if (activeSisa_18 < 0) {
            activeSisa_18 = 0;
        }
        $sb_18.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_18;
        
        activePerubahan_18 = activePerubahan_18 + $sb_18.adjust_menit;
        $sb_18.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_18;
        $sb_18.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb18._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_18.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_18.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_18.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_18.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_18.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb18._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_18.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_18 = ($sb18.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb18.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_18.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_18.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_18.mode_preheat || $sb_18.status_resep) {
                        $sb_18.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_18.mode_preheat && !$sb_18.status_resep && $sb_18.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_18 === 0 && !$sb_18.status_selesai && $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_18.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_18.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_18.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_18.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_18.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_18.status_kosong && !$sb_18.status_selesai && !$sb_18.mode_preheat && !$sb_18.status_resep) {
                        $sb_18.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_18.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_18.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_18.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_18.status_resep && activeSisa_18 === 0) {
                                $sb_18.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_18.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_18.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_18.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_18);
                        scale_up_18 = ((($sb_18.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_18) * 60) - activeSisa_18;
                        $sb_18.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_18 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_18);
                        if ($sb_18.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_18);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_18.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_18.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_18.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_18.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_18.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_18.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_18.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_18.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_18.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_18.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_18.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_18.suhu_awal = $sb18.temp;
                            activePerubahan_18 = 0;
                            $sb_18.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_18.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb18.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb18.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_18.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_18.suhu_akhir = $sb18.temp;
                            $sb_18.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_18.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_18.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_18.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_18.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_18.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_18.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_18 = $sb_18.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_18.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_18;
                            $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_18.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_18.suhu_awal = $sb18.temp;
                            activePerubahan_18 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_18.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb18.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_18.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_18.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_18.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_18.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_18.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_18);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_18 = ((($sb_18.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_18) * 60) - activeSisa_18) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_18;
                            $sb_18.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_18.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_18);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 18, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_18,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_18.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_18.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_18.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_18.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_18.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_18.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_18 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_18 = activeSisa_18 - 1;
                                $sb_18.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_18;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_18);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_18 = ((($sb_18.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_18) * 60) - activeSisa_18) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_18;
                            $sb_18.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_18 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_18 = 0;
                                $sb_18.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_18.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_18) * 60);
                                $sb_18.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb18.temp;
                                $sb_18.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb18.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_18.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_18.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_18.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 18;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.18;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.18;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.18;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.18;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.18;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.18;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.18;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_18.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_18.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_18.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_18.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_18; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_18.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_18.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_18);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 18, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_18,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_18.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_18.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_18) {
                    $sb_18.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb18.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_18.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_18.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_18.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_18.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_18.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_18.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_18.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_18.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_18.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_18.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_18.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 19
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_19.reset) {
    $sb_19.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_19.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_19.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_19.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_19.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_19.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_19.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_19.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_19.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_19.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_19.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_19.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.19 = "";
    $recipe_nama.19 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.19 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.19 = "";
    $recipe_qty.19 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.19 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.19 = "";
    
    $sb_19.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_19.status_resep = false;
    $sb_19.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_19.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_19.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_19.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_19 = 0;
    var activeSisa_19 = $sb_19.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_19 = $sb_19.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_19.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_19 = $sb_19.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_19 = activeSisa_19 + adjustSecs_19;
        if (activeSisa_19 < 0) {
            activeSisa_19 = 0;
        }
        $sb_19.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_19;
        
        activePerubahan_19 = activePerubahan_19 + $sb_19.adjust_menit;
        $sb_19.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_19;
        $sb_19.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb19._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_19.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_19.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_19.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_19.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_19.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb19._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_19.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_19 = ($sb19.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb19.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_19.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_19.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_19.mode_preheat || $sb_19.status_resep) {
                        $sb_19.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_19.mode_preheat && !$sb_19.status_resep && $sb_19.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_19 === 0 && !$sb_19.status_selesai && $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_19.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_19.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_19.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_19.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_19.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_19.status_kosong && !$sb_19.status_selesai && !$sb_19.mode_preheat && !$sb_19.status_resep) {
                        $sb_19.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_19.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_19.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_19.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_19.status_resep && activeSisa_19 === 0) {
                                $sb_19.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_19.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_19.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_19.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_19);
                        scale_up_19 = ((($sb_19.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_19) * 60) - activeSisa_19;
                        $sb_19.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_19 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_19);
                        if ($sb_19.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_19);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_19.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_19.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_19.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_19.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_19.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_19.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_19.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_19.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_19.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_19.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_19.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_19.suhu_awal = $sb19.temp;
                            activePerubahan_19 = 0;
                            $sb_19.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_19.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb19.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb19.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_19.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_19.suhu_akhir = $sb19.temp;
                            $sb_19.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_19.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_19.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_19.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_19.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_19.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_19.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_19 = $sb_19.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_19.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_19;
                            $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_19.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_19.suhu_awal = $sb19.temp;
                            activePerubahan_19 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_19.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb19.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_19.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_19.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_19.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_19.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_19.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_19);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_19 = ((($sb_19.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_19) * 60) - activeSisa_19) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_19;
                            $sb_19.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_19.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_19);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 19, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_19,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_19.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_19.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_19.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_19.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_19.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_19.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_19 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_19 = activeSisa_19 - 1;
                                $sb_19.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_19;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_19);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_19 = ((($sb_19.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_19) * 60) - activeSisa_19) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_19;
                            $sb_19.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_19 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_19 = 0;
                                $sb_19.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_19.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_19) * 60);
                                $sb_19.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb19.temp;
                                $sb_19.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb19.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_19.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_19.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_19.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 19;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.19;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.19;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.19;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.19;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.19;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.19;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.19;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_19.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_19.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_19.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_19.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_19; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_19.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_19.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_19);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 19, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_19,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_19.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_19.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_19) {
                    $sb_19.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb19.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_19.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_19.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_19.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_19.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_19.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_19.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_19.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_19.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_19.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_19.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_19.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 20
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_20.reset) {
    $sb_20.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_20.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_20.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_20.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_20.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_20.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_20.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_20.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_20.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_20.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_20.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_20.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.20 = "";
    $recipe_nama.20 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.20 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.20 = "";
    $recipe_qty.20 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.20 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.20 = "";
    
    $sb_20.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_20.status_resep = false;
    $sb_20.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_20.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_20.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_20.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_20 = 0;
    var activeSisa_20 = $sb_20.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_20 = $sb_20.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_20.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_20 = $sb_20.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_20 = activeSisa_20 + adjustSecs_20;
        if (activeSisa_20 < 0) {
            activeSisa_20 = 0;
        }
        $sb_20.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_20;
        
        activePerubahan_20 = activePerubahan_20 + $sb_20.adjust_menit;
        $sb_20.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_20;
        $sb_20.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb20._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_20.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_20.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_20.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_20.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_20.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb20._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_20.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_20 = ($sb20.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb20.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_20.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_20.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_20.mode_preheat || $sb_20.status_resep) {
                        $sb_20.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_20.mode_preheat && !$sb_20.status_resep && $sb_20.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_20 === 0 && !$sb_20.status_selesai && $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_20.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_20.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_20.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_20.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_20.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_20.status_kosong && !$sb_20.status_selesai && !$sb_20.mode_preheat && !$sb_20.status_resep) {
                        $sb_20.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_20.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_20.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_20.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_20.status_resep && activeSisa_20 === 0) {
                                $sb_20.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_20.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_20.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_20.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_20);
                        scale_up_20 = ((($sb_20.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_20) * 60) - activeSisa_20;
                        $sb_20.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_20 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_20);
                        if ($sb_20.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_20);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_20.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_20.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_20.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_20.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_20.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_20.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_20.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_20.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_20.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_20.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_20.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_20.suhu_awal = $sb20.temp;
                            activePerubahan_20 = 0;
                            $sb_20.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_20.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb20.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb20.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_20.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_20.suhu_akhir = $sb20.temp;
                            $sb_20.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_20.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_20.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_20.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_20.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_20.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_20.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_20 = $sb_20.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_20.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_20;
                            $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_20.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_20.suhu_awal = $sb20.temp;
                            activePerubahan_20 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_20.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb20.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_20.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_20.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_20.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_20.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_20.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_20);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_20 = ((($sb_20.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_20) * 60) - activeSisa_20) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_20;
                            $sb_20.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_20.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_20);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 20, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_20,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_20.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_20.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_20.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_20.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_20.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_20.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_20 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_20 = activeSisa_20 - 1;
                                $sb_20.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_20;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_20);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_20 = ((($sb_20.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_20) * 60) - activeSisa_20) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_20;
                            $sb_20.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_20 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_20 = 0;
                                $sb_20.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_20.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_20) * 60);
                                $sb_20.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb20.temp;
                                $sb_20.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb20.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_20.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_20.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_20.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 20;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.20;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.20;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.20;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.20;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.20;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.20;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.20;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_20.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_20.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_20.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_20.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_20; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_20.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_20.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_20);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 20, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_20,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_20.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_20.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_20) {
                    $sb_20.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb20.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_20.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_20.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_20.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_20.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_20.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_20.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_20.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_20.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_20.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_20.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_20.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 21
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_21.reset) {
    $sb_21.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_21.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_21.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_21.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_21.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_21.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_21.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_21.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_21.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_21.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_21.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_21.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.21 = "";
    $recipe_nama.21 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.21 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.21 = "";
    $recipe_qty.21 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.21 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.21 = "";
    
    $sb_21.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_21.status_resep = false;
    $sb_21.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_21.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_21.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_21.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_21 = 0;
    var activeSisa_21 = $sb_21.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_21 = $sb_21.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_21.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_21 = $sb_21.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_21 = activeSisa_21 + adjustSecs_21;
        if (activeSisa_21 < 0) {
            activeSisa_21 = 0;
        }
        $sb_21.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_21;
        
        activePerubahan_21 = activePerubahan_21 + $sb_21.adjust_menit;
        $sb_21.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_21;
        $sb_21.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb21._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_21.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_21.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_21.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_21.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_21.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb21._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_21.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_21 = ($sb21.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb21.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_21.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_21.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_21.mode_preheat || $sb_21.status_resep) {
                        $sb_21.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_21.mode_preheat && !$sb_21.status_resep && $sb_21.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_21 === 0 && !$sb_21.status_selesai && $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_21.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_21.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_21.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_21.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_21.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_21.status_kosong && !$sb_21.status_selesai && !$sb_21.mode_preheat && !$sb_21.status_resep) {
                        $sb_21.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_21.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_21.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_21.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_21.status_resep && activeSisa_21 === 0) {
                                $sb_21.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_21.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_21.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_21.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_21);
                        scale_up_21 = ((($sb_21.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_21) * 60) - activeSisa_21;
                        $sb_21.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_21 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_21);
                        if ($sb_21.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_21);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_21.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_21.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_21.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_21.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_21.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_21.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_21.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_21.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_21.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_21.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_21.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_21.suhu_awal = $sb21.temp;
                            activePerubahan_21 = 0;
                            $sb_21.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_21.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb21.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb21.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_21.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_21.suhu_akhir = $sb21.temp;
                            $sb_21.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_21.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_21.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_21.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_21.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_21.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_21.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_21 = $sb_21.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_21.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_21;
                            $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_21.flag_init_masak = 0;
