                            $sb_21.suhu_awal = $sb21.temp;
                            activePerubahan_21 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_21.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb21.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_21.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_21.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_21.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_21.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_21.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_21);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_21 = ((($sb_21.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_21) * 60) - activeSisa_21) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_21;
                            $sb_21.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_21.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_21);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 21, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_21,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_21.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_21.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_21.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_21.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_21.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_21.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_21 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_21 = activeSisa_21 - 1;
                                $sb_21.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_21;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_21);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_21 = ((($sb_21.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_21) * 60) - activeSisa_21) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_21;
                            $sb_21.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_21 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_21 = 0;
                                $sb_21.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_21.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_21) * 60);
                                $sb_21.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb21.temp;
                                $sb_21.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb21.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_21.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_21.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_21.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 21;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.21;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.21;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.21;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.21;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.21;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.21;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.21;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_21.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_21.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_21.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_21.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_21; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_21.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_21.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_21);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 21, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_21,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_21.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_21.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_21) {
                    $sb_21.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb21.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_21.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_21.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_21.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_21.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_21.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_21.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_21.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_21.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_21.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_21.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_21.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 22
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_22.reset) {
    $sb_22.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_22.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_22.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_22.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_22.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_22.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_22.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_22.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_22.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_22.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_22.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_22.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.22 = "";
    $recipe_nama.22 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.22 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.22 = "";
    $recipe_qty.22 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.22 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.22 = "";
    
    $sb_22.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_22.status_resep = false;
    $sb_22.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_22.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_22.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_22.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_22 = 0;
    var activeSisa_22 = $sb_22.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_22 = $sb_22.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_22.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_22 = $sb_22.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_22 = activeSisa_22 + adjustSecs_22;
        if (activeSisa_22 < 0) {
            activeSisa_22 = 0;
        }
        $sb_22.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_22;
        
        activePerubahan_22 = activePerubahan_22 + $sb_22.adjust_menit;
        $sb_22.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_22;
        $sb_22.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb22._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_22.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_22.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_22.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_22.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_22.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb22._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_22.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_22 = ($sb22.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb22.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_22.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_22.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_22.mode_preheat || $sb_22.status_resep) {
                        $sb_22.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_22.mode_preheat && !$sb_22.status_resep && $sb_22.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_22 === 0 && !$sb_22.status_selesai && $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_22.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_22.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_22.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_22.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_22.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_22.status_kosong && !$sb_22.status_selesai && !$sb_22.mode_preheat && !$sb_22.status_resep) {
                        $sb_22.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_22.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_22.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_22.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_22.status_resep && activeSisa_22 === 0) {
                                $sb_22.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_22.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_22.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_22.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_22);
                        scale_up_22 = ((($sb_22.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_22) * 60) - activeSisa_22;
                        $sb_22.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_22 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_22);
                        if ($sb_22.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_22);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_22.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_22.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_22.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_22.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_22.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_22.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_22.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_22.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_22.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_22.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_22.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_22.suhu_awal = $sb22.temp;
                            activePerubahan_22 = 0;
                            $sb_22.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_22.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb22.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb22.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_22.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_22.suhu_akhir = $sb22.temp;
                            $sb_22.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_22.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_22.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_22.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_22.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_22.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_22.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_22 = $sb_22.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_22.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_22;
                            $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_22.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_22.suhu_awal = $sb22.temp;
                            activePerubahan_22 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_22.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb22.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_22.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_22.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_22.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_22.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_22.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_22);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_22 = ((($sb_22.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_22) * 60) - activeSisa_22) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_22;
                            $sb_22.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_22.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_22);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 22, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_22,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_22.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_22.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_22.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_22.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_22.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_22.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_22 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_22 = activeSisa_22 - 1;
                                $sb_22.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_22;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_22);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_22 = ((($sb_22.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_22) * 60) - activeSisa_22) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_22;
                            $sb_22.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_22 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_22 = 0;
                                $sb_22.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_22.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_22) * 60);
                                $sb_22.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb22.temp;
                                $sb_22.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb22.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_22.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_22.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_22.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 22;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.22;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.22;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.22;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.22;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.22;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.22;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.22;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_22.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_22.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_22.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_22.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_22; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_22.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_22.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_22);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 22, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_22,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_22.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_22.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_22) {
                    $sb_22.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb22.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_22.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_22.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_22.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_22.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_22.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_22.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_22.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_22.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_22.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_22.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_22.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 23
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_23.reset) {
    $sb_23.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_23.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_23.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_23.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_23.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_23.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_23.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_23.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_23.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_23.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_23.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_23.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.23 = "";
    $recipe_nama.23 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.23 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.23 = "";
    $recipe_qty.23 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.23 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.23 = "";
    
    $sb_23.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_23.status_resep = false;
    $sb_23.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_23.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_23.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_23.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_23 = 0;
    var activeSisa_23 = $sb_23.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_23 = $sb_23.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_23.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_23 = $sb_23.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_23 = activeSisa_23 + adjustSecs_23;
        if (activeSisa_23 < 0) {
            activeSisa_23 = 0;
        }
        $sb_23.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_23;
        
        activePerubahan_23 = activePerubahan_23 + $sb_23.adjust_menit;
        $sb_23.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_23;
        $sb_23.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb23._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_23.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_23.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_23.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_23.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_23.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb23._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_23.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_23 = ($sb23.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb23.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_23.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_23.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_23.mode_preheat || $sb_23.status_resep) {
                        $sb_23.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_23.mode_preheat && !$sb_23.status_resep && $sb_23.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_23 === 0 && !$sb_23.status_selesai && $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_23.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_23.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_23.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_23.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_23.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_23.status_kosong && !$sb_23.status_selesai && !$sb_23.mode_preheat && !$sb_23.status_resep) {
                        $sb_23.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_23.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_23.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_23.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_23.status_resep && activeSisa_23 === 0) {
                                $sb_23.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_23.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_23.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_23.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_23);
                        scale_up_23 = ((($sb_23.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_23) * 60) - activeSisa_23;
                        $sb_23.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_23 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_23);
                        if ($sb_23.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_23);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_23.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_23.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_23.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_23.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_23.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_23.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_23.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_23.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_23.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_23.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_23.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_23.suhu_awal = $sb23.temp;
                            activePerubahan_23 = 0;
                            $sb_23.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_23.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb23.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb23.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_23.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_23.suhu_akhir = $sb23.temp;
                            $sb_23.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_23.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_23.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_23.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_23.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_23.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_23.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_23 = $sb_23.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_23.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_23;
                            $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_23.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_23.suhu_awal = $sb23.temp;
                            activePerubahan_23 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_23.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb23.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_23.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_23.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_23.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_23.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_23.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_23);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_23 = ((($sb_23.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_23) * 60) - activeSisa_23) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_23;
                            $sb_23.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_23.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_23);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 23, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_23,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_23.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_23.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_23.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_23.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_23.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_23.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_23 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_23 = activeSisa_23 - 1;
                                $sb_23.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_23;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_23);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_23 = ((($sb_23.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_23) * 60) - activeSisa_23) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_23;
                            $sb_23.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_23 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_23 = 0;
                                $sb_23.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_23.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_23) * 60);
                                $sb_23.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb23.temp;
                                $sb_23.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb23.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_23.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_23.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_23.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 23;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.23;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.23;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.23;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.23;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.23;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.23;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.23;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_23.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_23.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_23.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_23.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_23; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_23.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_23.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_23);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 23, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_23,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_23.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_23.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_23) {
                    $sb_23.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb23.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_23.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_23.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_23.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_23.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_23.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_23.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_23.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_23.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_23.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_23.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_23.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 24
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_24.reset) {
    $sb_24.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_24.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_24.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_24.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_24.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_24.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_24.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_24.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_24.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_24.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_24.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_24.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.24 = "";
    $recipe_nama.24 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.24 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.24 = "";
    $recipe_qty.24 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.24 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.24 = "";
    
    $sb_24.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_24.status_resep = false;
    $sb_24.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_24.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_24.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_24.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_24 = 0;
    var activeSisa_24 = $sb_24.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_24 = $sb_24.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_24.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_24 = $sb_24.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_24 = activeSisa_24 + adjustSecs_24;
        if (activeSisa_24 < 0) {
            activeSisa_24 = 0;
        }
        $sb_24.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_24;
        
        activePerubahan_24 = activePerubahan_24 + $sb_24.adjust_menit;
        $sb_24.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_24;
        $sb_24.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb24._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_24.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_24.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_24.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_24.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_24.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb24._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_24.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_24 = ($sb24.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb24.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_24.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_24.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_24.mode_preheat || $sb_24.status_resep) {
                        $sb_24.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_24.mode_preheat && !$sb_24.status_resep && $sb_24.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_24 === 0 && !$sb_24.status_selesai && $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_24.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_24.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_24.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_24.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_24.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_24.status_kosong && !$sb_24.status_selesai && !$sb_24.mode_preheat && !$sb_24.status_resep) {
                        $sb_24.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_24.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_24.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_24.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_24.status_resep && activeSisa_24 === 0) {
                                $sb_24.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_24.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_24.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_24.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_24);
                        scale_up_24 = ((($sb_24.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_24) * 60) - activeSisa_24;
                        $sb_24.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_24 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_24);
                        if ($sb_24.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_24);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_24.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_24.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_24.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_24.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_24.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_24.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_24.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_24.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_24.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_24.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_24.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_24.suhu_awal = $sb24.temp;
                            activePerubahan_24 = 0;
                            $sb_24.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_24.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb24.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb24.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_24.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_24.suhu_akhir = $sb24.temp;
                            $sb_24.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_24.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_24.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_24.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_24.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_24.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_24.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_24 = $sb_24.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_24.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_24;
                            $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_24.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_24.suhu_awal = $sb24.temp;
                            activePerubahan_24 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_24.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb24.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_24.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_24.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_24.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_24.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_24.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_24);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_24 = ((($sb_24.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_24) * 60) - activeSisa_24) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_24;
                            $sb_24.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_24.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_24);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 24, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_24,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_24.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_24.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_24.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_24.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_24.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_24.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_24 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_24 = activeSisa_24 - 1;
                                $sb_24.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_24;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_24);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_24 = ((($sb_24.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_24) * 60) - activeSisa_24) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_24;
                            $sb_24.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_24 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_24 = 0;
                                $sb_24.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_24.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_24) * 60);
                                $sb_24.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb24.temp;
                                $sb_24.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb24.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_24.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_24.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_24.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 24;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.24;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.24;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.24;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.24;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.24;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.24;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.24;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_24.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_24.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_24.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_24.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_24; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_24.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_24.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_24);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 24, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_24,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_24.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_24.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_24) {
                    $sb_24.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb24.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_24.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_24.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_24.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_24.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_24.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_24.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_24.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_24.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_24.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_24.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_24.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 25
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_25.reset) {
    $sb_25.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_25.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_25.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_25.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_25.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_25.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_25.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_25.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_25.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_25.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_25.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_25.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.25 = "";
    $recipe_nama.25 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.25 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.25 = "";
    $recipe_qty.25 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.25 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.25 = "";
    
    $sb_25.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_25.status_resep = false;
    $sb_25.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_25.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_25.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_25.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_25 = 0;
    var activeSisa_25 = $sb_25.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_25 = $sb_25.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_25.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_25 = $sb_25.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_25 = activeSisa_25 + adjustSecs_25;
        if (activeSisa_25 < 0) {
            activeSisa_25 = 0;
        }
        $sb_25.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_25;
        
        activePerubahan_25 = activePerubahan_25 + $sb_25.adjust_menit;
        $sb_25.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_25;
        $sb_25.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb25._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_25.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_25.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_25.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_25.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_25.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb25._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_25.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_25 = ($sb25.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb25.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_25.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_25.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_25.mode_preheat || $sb_25.status_resep) {
                        $sb_25.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_25.mode_preheat && !$sb_25.status_resep && $sb_25.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_25 === 0 && !$sb_25.status_selesai && $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_25.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_25.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_25.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_25.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_25.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_25.status_kosong && !$sb_25.status_selesai && !$sb_25.mode_preheat && !$sb_25.status_resep) {
                        $sb_25.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_25.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_25.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_25.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_25.status_resep && activeSisa_25 === 0) {
                                $sb_25.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_25.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_25.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_25.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_25);
                        scale_up_25 = ((($sb_25.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_25) * 60) - activeSisa_25;
                        $sb_25.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_25 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_25);
                        if ($sb_25.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_25);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_25.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_25.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_25.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_25.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_25.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_25.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_25.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_25.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_25.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_25.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_25.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_25.suhu_awal = $sb25.temp;
                            activePerubahan_25 = 0;
                            $sb_25.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_25.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb25.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb25.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_25.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_25.suhu_akhir = $sb25.temp;
                            $sb_25.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_25.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_25.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_25.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_25.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_25.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_25.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_25 = $sb_25.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_25.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_25;
                            $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_25.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_25.suhu_awal = $sb25.temp;
                            activePerubahan_25 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_25.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb25.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_25.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_25.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_25.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_25.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_25.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_25);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_25 = ((($sb_25.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_25) * 60) - activeSisa_25) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_25;
                            $sb_25.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_25.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_25);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 25, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_25,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_25.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_25.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_25.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_25.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_25.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_25.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_25 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_25 = activeSisa_25 - 1;
                                $sb_25.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_25;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_25);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_25 = ((($sb_25.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_25) * 60) - activeSisa_25) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_25;
                            $sb_25.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_25 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_25 = 0;
                                $sb_25.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_25.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_25) * 60);
                                $sb_25.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb25.temp;
                                $sb_25.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb25.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_25.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_25.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_25.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 25;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.25;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.25;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.25;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.25;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.25;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.25;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.25;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_25.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_25.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_25.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_25.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_25; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_25.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_25.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_25);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 25, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_25,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_25.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_25.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_25) {
                    $sb_25.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb25.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_25.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_25.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_25.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_25.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_25.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_25.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_25.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_25.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_25.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_25.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_25.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 26
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_26.reset) {
    $sb_26.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_26.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_26.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_26.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_26.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_26.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_26.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_26.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_26.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_26.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_26.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_26.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.26 = "";
    $recipe_nama.26 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.26 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.26 = "";
    $recipe_qty.26 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.26 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.26 = "";
    
    $sb_26.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_26.status_resep = false;
    $sb_26.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_26.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_26.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_26.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_26 = 0;
    var activeSisa_26 = $sb_26.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_26 = $sb_26.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_26.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_26 = $sb_26.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_26 = activeSisa_26 + adjustSecs_26;
        if (activeSisa_26 < 0) {
            activeSisa_26 = 0;
        }
        $sb_26.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_26;
        
        activePerubahan_26 = activePerubahan_26 + $sb_26.adjust_menit;
        $sb_26.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_26;
        $sb_26.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb26._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_26.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_26.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_26.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_26.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_26.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb26._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_26.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_26 = ($sb26.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb26.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_26.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_26.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_26.mode_preheat || $sb_26.status_resep) {
                        $sb_26.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_26.mode_preheat && !$sb_26.status_resep && $sb_26.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_26 === 0 && !$sb_26.status_selesai && $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_26.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_26.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_26.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_26.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_26.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_26.status_kosong && !$sb_26.status_selesai && !$sb_26.mode_preheat && !$sb_26.status_resep) {
                        $sb_26.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_26.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_26.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_26.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_26.status_resep && activeSisa_26 === 0) {
                                $sb_26.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_26.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_26.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_26.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_26);
                        scale_up_26 = ((($sb_26.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_26) * 60) - activeSisa_26;
                        $sb_26.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_26 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_26);
                        if ($sb_26.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_26);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_26.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_26.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_26.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_26.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_26.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_26.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_26.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_26.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_26.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_26.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_26.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_26.suhu_awal = $sb26.temp;
                            activePerubahan_26 = 0;
                            $sb_26.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_26.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb26.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb26.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_26.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_26.suhu_akhir = $sb26.temp;
                            $sb_26.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_26.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_26.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_26.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_26.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_26.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_26.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_26 = $sb_26.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_26.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_26;
                            $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_26.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_26.suhu_awal = $sb26.temp;
                            activePerubahan_26 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_26.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb26.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_26.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_26.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_26.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_26.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_26.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_26);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_26 = ((($sb_26.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_26) * 60) - activeSisa_26) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_26;
                            $sb_26.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_26.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_26);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 26, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_26,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_26.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_26.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_26.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
