                            if ($sb_26.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_26.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_26.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_26 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_26 = activeSisa_26 - 1;
                                $sb_26.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_26;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_26);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_26 = ((($sb_26.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_26) * 60) - activeSisa_26) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_26;
                            $sb_26.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_26 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_26 = 0;
                                $sb_26.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_26.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_26) * 60);
                                $sb_26.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb26.temp;
                                $sb_26.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb26.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_26.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_26.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_26.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 26;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.26;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.26;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.26;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.26;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.26;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.26;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.26;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_26.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_26.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_26.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_26.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_26; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_26.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_26.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_26);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 26, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_26,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_26.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_26.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_26) {
                    $sb_26.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb26.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_26.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_26.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_26.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_26.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_26.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_26.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_26.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_26.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_26.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_26.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_26.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 27
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_27.reset) {
    $sb_27.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_27.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_27.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_27.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_27.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_27.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_27.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_27.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_27.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_27.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_27.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_27.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.27 = "";
    $recipe_nama.27 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.27 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.27 = "";
    $recipe_qty.27 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.27 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.27 = "";
    
    $sb_27.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_27.status_resep = false;
    $sb_27.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_27.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_27.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_27.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_27 = 0;
    var activeSisa_27 = $sb_27.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_27 = $sb_27.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_27.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_27 = $sb_27.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_27 = activeSisa_27 + adjustSecs_27;
        if (activeSisa_27 < 0) {
            activeSisa_27 = 0;
        }
        $sb_27.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_27;
        
        activePerubahan_27 = activePerubahan_27 + $sb_27.adjust_menit;
        $sb_27.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_27;
        $sb_27.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb27._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_27.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_27.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_27.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_27.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_27.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb27._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_27.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_27 = ($sb27.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb27.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_27.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_27.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_27.mode_preheat || $sb_27.status_resep) {
                        $sb_27.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_27.mode_preheat && !$sb_27.status_resep && $sb_27.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_27 === 0 && !$sb_27.status_selesai && $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_27.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_27.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_27.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_27.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_27.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_27.status_kosong && !$sb_27.status_selesai && !$sb_27.mode_preheat && !$sb_27.status_resep) {
                        $sb_27.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_27.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_27.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_27.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_27.status_resep && activeSisa_27 === 0) {
                                $sb_27.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_27.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_27.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_27.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_27);
                        scale_up_27 = ((($sb_27.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_27) * 60) - activeSisa_27;
                        $sb_27.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_27 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_27);
                        if ($sb_27.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_27);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_27.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_27.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_27.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_27.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_27.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_27.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_27.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_27.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_27.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_27.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_27.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_27.suhu_awal = $sb27.temp;
                            activePerubahan_27 = 0;
                            $sb_27.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_27.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb27.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb27.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_27.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_27.suhu_akhir = $sb27.temp;
                            $sb_27.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_27.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_27.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_27.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_27.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_27.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_27.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_27 = $sb_27.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_27.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_27;
                            $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_27.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_27.suhu_awal = $sb27.temp;
                            activePerubahan_27 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_27.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb27.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_27.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_27.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_27.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_27.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_27.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_27);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_27 = ((($sb_27.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_27) * 60) - activeSisa_27) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_27;
                            $sb_27.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_27.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_27);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 27, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_27,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_27.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_27.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_27.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_27.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_27.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_27.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_27 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_27 = activeSisa_27 - 1;
                                $sb_27.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_27;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_27);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_27 = ((($sb_27.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_27) * 60) - activeSisa_27) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_27;
                            $sb_27.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_27 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_27 = 0;
                                $sb_27.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_27.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_27) * 60);
                                $sb_27.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb27.temp;
                                $sb_27.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb27.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_27.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_27.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_27.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 27;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.27;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.27;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.27;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.27;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.27;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.27;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.27;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_27.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_27.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_27.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_27.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_27; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_27.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_27.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_27);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 27, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_27,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_27.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_27.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_27) {
                    $sb_27.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb27.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_27.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_27.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_27.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_27.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_27.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_27.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_27.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_27.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_27.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_27.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_27.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 28
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_28.reset) {
    $sb_28.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_28.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_28.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_28.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_28.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_28.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_28.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_28.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_28.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_28.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_28.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_28.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.28 = "";
    $recipe_nama.28 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.28 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.28 = "";
    $recipe_qty.28 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.28 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.28 = "";
    
    $sb_28.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_28.status_resep = false;
    $sb_28.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_28.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_28.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_28.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_28 = 0;
    var activeSisa_28 = $sb_28.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_28 = $sb_28.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_28.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_28 = $sb_28.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_28 = activeSisa_28 + adjustSecs_28;
        if (activeSisa_28 < 0) {
            activeSisa_28 = 0;
        }
        $sb_28.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_28;
        
        activePerubahan_28 = activePerubahan_28 + $sb_28.adjust_menit;
        $sb_28.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_28;
        $sb_28.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb28._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_28.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_28.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_28.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_28.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_28.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb28._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_28.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_28 = ($sb28.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb28.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_28.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_28.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_28.mode_preheat || $sb_28.status_resep) {
                        $sb_28.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_28.mode_preheat && !$sb_28.status_resep && $sb_28.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_28 === 0 && !$sb_28.status_selesai && $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_28.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_28.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_28.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_28.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_28.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_28.status_kosong && !$sb_28.status_selesai && !$sb_28.mode_preheat && !$sb_28.status_resep) {
                        $sb_28.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_28.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_28.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_28.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_28.status_resep && activeSisa_28 === 0) {
                                $sb_28.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_28.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_28.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_28.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_28);
                        scale_up_28 = ((($sb_28.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_28) * 60) - activeSisa_28;
                        $sb_28.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_28 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_28);
                        if ($sb_28.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_28);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_28.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_28.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_28.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_28.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_28.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_28.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_28.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_28.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_28.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_28.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_28.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_28.suhu_awal = $sb28.temp;
                            activePerubahan_28 = 0;
                            $sb_28.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_28.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb28.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb28.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_28.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_28.suhu_akhir = $sb28.temp;
                            $sb_28.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_28.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_28.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_28.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_28.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_28.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_28.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_28 = $sb_28.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_28.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_28;
                            $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_28.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_28.suhu_awal = $sb28.temp;
                            activePerubahan_28 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_28.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb28.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_28.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_28.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_28.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_28.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_28.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_28);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_28 = ((($sb_28.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_28) * 60) - activeSisa_28) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_28;
                            $sb_28.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_28.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_28);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 28, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_28,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_28.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_28.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_28.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_28.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_28.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_28.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_28 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_28 = activeSisa_28 - 1;
                                $sb_28.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_28;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_28);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_28 = ((($sb_28.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_28) * 60) - activeSisa_28) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_28;
                            $sb_28.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_28 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_28 = 0;
                                $sb_28.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_28.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_28) * 60);
                                $sb_28.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb28.temp;
                                $sb_28.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb28.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_28.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_28.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_28.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 28;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.28;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.28;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.28;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.28;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.28;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.28;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.28;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_28.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_28.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_28.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_28.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_28; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_28.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_28.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_28);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 28, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_28,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_28.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_28.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_28) {
                    $sb_28.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb28.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_28.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_28.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_28.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_28.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_28.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_28.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_28.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_28.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_28.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_28.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_28.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 29
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_29.reset) {
    $sb_29.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_29.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_29.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_29.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_29.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_29.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_29.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_29.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_29.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_29.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_29.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_29.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.29 = "";
    $recipe_nama.29 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.29 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.29 = "";
    $recipe_qty.29 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.29 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.29 = "";
    
    $sb_29.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_29.status_resep = false;
    $sb_29.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_29.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_29.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_29.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_29 = 0;
    var activeSisa_29 = $sb_29.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_29 = $sb_29.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_29.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_29 = $sb_29.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_29 = activeSisa_29 + adjustSecs_29;
        if (activeSisa_29 < 0) {
            activeSisa_29 = 0;
        }
        $sb_29.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_29;
        
        activePerubahan_29 = activePerubahan_29 + $sb_29.adjust_menit;
        $sb_29.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_29;
        $sb_29.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb29._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_29.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_29.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_29.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_29.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_29.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb29._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_29.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_29 = ($sb29.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb29.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_29.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_29.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_29.mode_preheat || $sb_29.status_resep) {
                        $sb_29.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_29.mode_preheat && !$sb_29.status_resep && $sb_29.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_29 === 0 && !$sb_29.status_selesai && $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_29.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_29.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_29.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_29.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_29.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_29.status_kosong && !$sb_29.status_selesai && !$sb_29.mode_preheat && !$sb_29.status_resep) {
                        $sb_29.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_29.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_29.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_29.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_29.status_resep && activeSisa_29 === 0) {
                                $sb_29.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_29.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_29.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_29.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_29);
                        scale_up_29 = ((($sb_29.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_29) * 60) - activeSisa_29;
                        $sb_29.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_29 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_29);
                        if ($sb_29.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_29);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_29.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_29.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_29.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_29.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_29.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_29.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_29.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_29.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_29.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_29.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_29.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_29.suhu_awal = $sb29.temp;
                            activePerubahan_29 = 0;
                            $sb_29.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_29.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb29.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb29.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_29.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_29.suhu_akhir = $sb29.temp;
                            $sb_29.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_29.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_29.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_29.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_29.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_29.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_29.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_29 = $sb_29.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_29.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_29;
                            $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_29.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_29.suhu_awal = $sb29.temp;
                            activePerubahan_29 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_29.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb29.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_29.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_29.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_29.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_29.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_29.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_29);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_29 = ((($sb_29.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_29) * 60) - activeSisa_29) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_29;
                            $sb_29.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_29.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_29);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 29, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_29,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_29.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_29.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_29.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_29.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_29.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_29.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_29 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_29 = activeSisa_29 - 1;
                                $sb_29.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_29;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_29);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_29 = ((($sb_29.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_29) * 60) - activeSisa_29) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_29;
                            $sb_29.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_29 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_29 = 0;
                                $sb_29.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_29.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_29) * 60);
                                $sb_29.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb29.temp;
                                $sb_29.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb29.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_29.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_29.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_29.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 29;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.29;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.29;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.29;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.29;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.29;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.29;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.29;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_29.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_29.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_29.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_29.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_29; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_29.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_29.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_29);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 29, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_29,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_29.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_29.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_29) {
                    $sb_29.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb29.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_29.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_29.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_29.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_29.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_29.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_29.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_29.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_29.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_29.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_29.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_29.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}

// ==========================================
// STEAMBOX UNIT 30
// ==========================================
// 1. Trigger reset khusus Tugas Baru / Reset (Berdiri sendiri di luar komunikasi/logic)
if ($sb_30.reset) {
    $sb_30.status_selesai = false;
    $sb_30.flag_init_masak = 0;
    $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
    $sb_30.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
    $sb_30.target_menit = 0;
    $sb_30.adjust_menit = 0;
    $sb_30.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_30.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
    $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
    $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
    $sb_30.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
    $sb_30.tampil_pemanasan = "--:--:--";
    $sb_30.suhu_awal = 0;
    $sb_30.suhu_akhir = 0;
    $sb_30.perubahan_waktu = 0;
    
    $recipe_kode.30 = "";
    $recipe_nama.30 = "--";
    $recipe_versi.30 = 0;
    $recipe_warna.30 = "";
    $recipe_qty.30 = 0;
    $recipe_batch.30 = 0;
    $recipe_trolly.30 = "";
    
    $sb_30.status_kosong = true;
    $sb_30.status_resep = false;
    $sb_30.mode_preheat = false;
    $sb_30.flag_init_start = 0;
    $sb_30.status_banner = txtKosong;
    $sb_30.reset = false; // matikan trigger reset
}
else {
    var scale_up_30 = 0;
    var activeSisa_30 = $sb_30.sisa_detik_masak || 0;
    var activePerubahan_30 = $sb_30.perubahan_waktu || 0;
    
    if ($sb_30.adjust_menit !== 0) {
        var adjustSecs_30 = $sb_30.adjust_menit * 60;
        activeSisa_30 = activeSisa_30 + adjustSecs_30;
        if (activeSisa_30 < 0) {
            activeSisa_30 = 0;
        }
        $sb_30.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_30;
        
        activePerubahan_30 = activePerubahan_30 + $sb_30.adjust_menit;
        $sb_30.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_30;
        $sb_30.adjust_menit = 0;
    }

    if (!$sb30._commOperation) { // UNIT TIDAK DIPAKAI (Disabled)
        $sb_30.status_banner = txtDisable;
        $sb_30.status_pemanasan = false;
        $sb_30.status_pemasakan = false;
        $sb_30.status_selesai = false;
        $sb_30.sensor_error = false;
    } else {
        if ($sb30._commStatus) { // CONNECTED
            if (!$sb_30.maintenance_mode) {
                var isSensorError_30 = ($sb30.temp >= tempErrorLimit);
                
                if (Number($sb30.run_stop) === 1) { // STOPPED / PAUSED
                    $sb_30.status_pemanasan = false;
                    $sb_30.status_pemasakan = false;
                    
                    // Jika operator memilih preheat atau mentransfer resep, tangki tidak kosong lagi
                    if ($sb_30.mode_preheat || $sb_30.status_resep) {
                        $sb_30.status_kosong = false;
                    }
                    
                    // Enforce status_kosong jika berada di kondisi standby default (dan preheat belum pernah jalan)
                    if (!$sb_30.mode_preheat && !$sb_30.status_resep && $sb_30.target_menit === 0 && activeSisa_30 === 0 && !$sb_30.status_selesai && $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                        $sb_30.status_kosong = true;
                    }
                    
                    if ($sb_30.status_kosong) {
                        $sb_30.status_banner = txtKosong;
                    } else if ($sb_30.status_selesai) {
                        $sb_30.status_banner = txtSelesai;
                    } else if (!$sb_30.status_kosong && !$sb_30.status_selesai && !$sb_30.mode_preheat && !$sb_30.status_resep) {
                        $sb_30.status_banner = txtSelesaiPreheat;
                    } else {
                        if ($sb_30.mode_preheat) {
                            if ($sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan === 0) {
                                $sb_30.status_banner = txtSiapPreheat;
                            } else {
                                $sb_30.status_banner = txtPreheatPaused;
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ($sb_30.status_resep && activeSisa_30 === 0) {
                                $sb_30.status_banner = txtStatusResep;
                            } else {
                                $sb_30.status_banner = txtPaused;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Locked update jika status_selesai sudah ON
                    if ($sb_30.flag_init_start === 1 && Number($sb_30.status_selesai) === 0) {
                        $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_30);
                        scale_up_30 = ((($sb_30.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_30) * 60) - activeSisa_30;
                        $sb_30.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(scale_up_30 < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_30);
                        if ($sb_30.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                            $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_30);
                        }
                    }
                } else { // RUNNING
                    $sb_30.status_kosong = false;
                    
                    if ($sb_30.mode_preheat) { // PRE-HEAT MODE (Hanya durasi pemanasan yang berjalan, jam mulai/masak/selesai tetap "--:--:--")
                        $sb_30.status_pemanasan = false;
                        $sb_30.status_pemasakan = false;
                        $sb_30.status_banner = txtPreheat;
                        
                        if ($sb_30.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_30.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_30.tampil_jam_mulai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_30.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual = "--";
                            $sb_30.durasi_aktual_up = "--";
                            $sb_30.flag_init_start = 1;
                            $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_30.suhu_awal = $sb30.temp;
                            activePerubahan_30 = 0;
                            $sb_30.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                        $sb_30.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan);
                        
                        if ($sb30.temp > 1000) {
                            $sb30.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                            $sb_30.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_30.suhu_akhir = $sb30.temp;
                            $sb_30.flag_init_start = 0;
                            $sb_30.mode_preheat = false; // Balikkan mode_preheat otomatis ke false
                        }
                    } else { // COOKING MODE
                        if ($sb_30.flag_init_start === 0) {
                            $sb_30.status_selesai = false; // Auto-reset status selesai saat batch baru mulai
                            $sb_30.tampil_jam_mulai = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam mulai sekali
                            $sb_30.tampil_jam_masak = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            $sb_30.flag_init_start = 1;
                            activeSisa_30 = $sb_30.target_menit * 60;
                            $sb_30.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_30;
                            $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan = 0;
                            $sb_30.flag_init_masak = 0;
                            $sb_30.suhu_awal = $sb30.temp;
                            activePerubahan_30 = 0; // perubahan_waktu dimulai dari 0
                            $sb_30.perubahan_waktu = 0;
                        }
                        
                        if ($sb30.temp < 1000) { // Heating (< 100 C): Jam mulai dicatat, jam masak & selesai tetap "--:--:--", durasi aktual up mulai hitung naik
                            $sb_30.status_pemanasan = true;
                            $sb_30.status_pemasakan = false;
                            $sb_30.status_banner = txtPemanasan; // Tunggu mendidih
                            $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan = $sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan + 1;
                            $sb_30.tampil_pemanasan = formatTime($sb_30.total_detik_pemanasan);
                            
                            $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_30);
                            var detik_up_heat = (scale_up_30 = ((($sb_30.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_30) * 60) - activeSisa_30) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_30;
                            $sb_30.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_heat);
                            
                            // Jika sebelumnya sudah pernah mendidih (mengalami drop temp), jam selesai bertambah dan tetap tampil di monitor
                            if ($sb_30.flag_init_masak === 1) {
                                $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_30);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 30, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_30,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            } else {
                                $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = "--:--:--";
                            }
                        } else { // Boiling (>= 100 C): Jam masak & selesai dicatat, durasi aktual mulai hitung mundur
                            $sb_30.status_pemanasan = false;
                            $sb_30.status_pemasakan = true;
                            $sb_30.status_banner = txtPemasakan;
                            
                            if ($sb_30.flag_init_masak === 0) {
                                $sb_30.tampil_jam_masak = waktuSekarangString; // Catat jam masak sekali
                                $sb_30.flag_init_masak = 1;
                            }
                            
                            if (activeSisa_30 > 0) {
                                activeSisa_30 = activeSisa_30 - 1;
                                $sb_30.sisa_detik_masak = activeSisa_30;
                            }
                            
                            $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(activeSisa_30);
                            var detik_up_boil = (scale_up_30 = ((($sb_30.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_30) * 60) - activeSisa_30) < 0 ? 0 : scale_up_30;
                            $sb_30.durasi_aktual_up = formatTime(detik_up_boil);
                            
                            if (activeSisa_30 <= 0) {
                                activeSisa_30 = 0;
                                $sb_30.sisa_detik_masak = 0;
                                $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual = formatTime(0);
                                
                                var finalDurasiUpStr = formatTime((($sb_30.target_menit || 0) + activePerubahan_30) * 60);
                                $sb_30.durasi_aktual_up = finalDurasiUpStr;
                                
                                var finalJamSelesaiStr = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, 0);
                                $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr;
                                
                                var finalSuhuAkhir = $sb30.temp;
                                $sb_30.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir;
                                
                                $sb30.run_stop = 1; // STOP otomatis
                                $sb_30.status_pemasakan = false;
                                $sb_30.flag_init_start = 0;
                                $sb_30.flag_init_masak = 0;
                                
                                // === TRANSFER DATA SELESAI KE data_group_master (DENGAN VARIABEL LOKAL) ===
                                $data_group_master.no_steambox = 30;
                                $data_group_master.kode = $recipe_kode.30;
                                $data_group_master.nama = $recipe_nama.30;
                                $data_group_master.versi = $recipe_versi.30;
                                $data_group_master.batch = $recipe_batch.30;
                                $data_group_master.warna = $recipe_warna.30;
                                $data_group_master.qty = $recipe_qty.30;
                                $data_group_master.trolly = $recipe_trolly.30;
                                $data_group_master.durasi = $sb_30.target_menit;
                                $data_group_master.jam_mulai = $sb_30.tampil_jam_mulai;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_pemanasan = $sb_30.tampil_pemanasan;
                                $data_group_master.jam_masak = $sb_30.tampil_jam_masak;
                                $data_group_master.durasi_aktual = finalDurasiUpStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.jam_selesai = finalJamSelesaiStr; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.perubahan_waktu = activePerubahan_30; // Kirim akumulasi adjust_menit ril
                                $data_group_master.suhu_awal = $sb_30.suhu_awal;
                                $data_group_master.suhu_akhir = finalSuhuAkhir; // Tulis langsung dari variabel lokal
                                $data_group_master.status = "SUCCESS";

                                // Trigger global Data Group log
                                $Sys_Control.trigger_log = true;

                                $sb_30.status_selesai = true;
                            } else {
                                $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai = getEstimasiSelesai(totalDetikSekarang, activeSisa_30);
                                runningRooms.push({
                                    name: 30, // Hanya nomor Steambox saja
                                    sisa: activeSisa_30,
                                    tampilSisa: $sb_30.tampil_durasi_aktual,
                                    tampilSelesai: $sb_30.tampil_jam_selesai
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // 3. Alarm Sensor Error (Kritis)
                if (isSensorError_30) {
                    $sb_30.sensor_error = true;
                    if (Number($sb30.run_stop) === 0 && $sb_30.flag_init_start === 1) {
                        $sb_30.status_banner = txtSensorErrorCooking;
                    } else {
                        $sb_30.status_banner = txtSensorError;
                    }
                } else {
                    $sb_30.sensor_error = false;
                }
            } else { // MODE MAINTENANCE (KONTROL MANUAL)
                $sb_30.status_banner = txtMaintenance;
                $sb_30.sensor_error = false;
            }
        } else { // DEVICE OFFLINE (Gagal Komunikasi)
            $sb_30.status_banner = txtOffline;
            $sb_30.status_pemanasan = false;
            $sb_30.status_pemasakan = false;
            $sb_30.status_selesai = false;
            $sb_30.sensor_error = false;
        }
    }
}
// ==========================================
// 4. SORTING MONITOR LUAR (TOP 5)
// ==========================================
runningRooms.sort(function(a, b) {
    return a.sisa - b.sisa;
});

// Slot 1
if (runningRooms.length >= 1) {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_1 = runningRooms[0].name;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_1 = runningRooms[0].tampilSisa;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_1 = runningRooms[0].tampilSelesai;
} else {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_1 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_1 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_1 = "--";
}

// Slot 2
if (runningRooms.length >= 2) {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_2 = runningRooms[1].name;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_2 = runningRooms[1].tampilSisa;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_2 = runningRooms[1].tampilSelesai;
} else {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_2 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_2 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_2 = "--";
}

// Slot 3
if (runningRooms.length >= 3) {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_3 = runningRooms[2].name;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_3 = runningRooms[2].tampilSisa;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_3 = runningRooms[2].tampilSelesai;
} else {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_3 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_3 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_3 = "--";
}

// Slot 4
if (runningRooms.length >= 4) {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_4 = runningRooms[3].name;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_4 = runningRooms[3].tampilSisa;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_4 = runningRooms[3].tampilSelesai;
} else {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_4 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_4 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_4 = "--";
}

// Slot 5
if (runningRooms.length >= 5) {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_5 = runningRooms[4].name;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_5 = runningRooms[4].tampilSisa;
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_5 = runningRooms[4].tampilSelesai;
} else {
    $Sys_Control.monitor_room_5 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_sisa_5 = "--";
    $Sys_Control.monitor_selesai_5 = "--";
}
